In any case, the Chinese Eastern Railway negotiations have now reached the final stage. There must be one of two outcomes: either a peaceful resolution or the breakdown of the conference. Japan and "Manchukuo" are now awaiting a reply telegram from Moscow to determine the final solution. (Dispatch of the 25th, Reuters)

Roosevelt Arrives in Honolulu 34

Honolulu The cruiser Houston, carrying US President Roosevelt, arrived in Kailua Bay, Hawaii, today. The Governor of Honolulu will give an official welcome to the US head of state's visit, and the people of Hawaii will also provide various entertainments, preparing to hold canoe races, and native dances and concerts to entertain him, and will show the state of life of the natives before the arrival of white people (Reuters telegram of the 24th) Siam's Abundant Resources Not Yet Developed Becoming a Hunting Ground for Britain and Japan

Britain and France both want to guarantee its independence as a buffer between their colonies Siam seeks assistance from London to expand its navy 35

Bangkok Siam has many undeveloped resources, and now it has become a hunting ground for commercial battles between Britain and Japan. Japanese goods are crowding out Western goods in the Siamese market, gradually pushing them out. In this regard, the most severely affected is Britain. The commercial relationship between France and Siam is not very important, and there is no conflict between French manufactured goods imported into Siam and Japanese goods. Political observers believe that this is the reason why France and Japan can be friendly. Recently, the Siamese Consul-General in Singapore was downgraded to Consul, while the Japanese side was promoted to Consul-General. Agile British politicians immediately invited the King and Queen of Siam to visit Britain as a counterbalance. London newspapers reported that what Siam needs is a larger navy to defend against Japanese attacks. The purpose of the Siamese King's visit to Britain this time is to negotiate this matter. However, political observers believe that Siam does not need to fear Japanese aggression, because Britain and France both want to guarantee Siam's independence as a buffer between their territories. (National Telegram of the 25th)

The Future Great War Will Be Decided by Air Force American Squadron Flight Completes Half the Journey to Alaska to Test Its Power

Japan Urgently Catches Up and Attempts Long-Distance Flight Between Japan and Taiwan 36

Whitehorse A squadron of US Army bombers is currently flying in formation to test the ability of the US Army to defend Alaska, and will depart from here this morning for Fairbanks, Alaska. (Reuters telegram of the 24th)

Fairbanks Ten Martin bombers of the Army squadron flight landed here today, having completed half of the round trip flight between Washington and Fairbanks. The Army flying squadron took off from the Bolling Field in Washington, D.C. on Thursday morning, a journey of about 4,000 miles. The speed of the flight was unexpected. It has not yet been announced when they will depart to fly back. The purpose of this flight is obviously to give the pilots long-distance flight training, and to practice photography in Alaska, while testing the power of the Martin bombers, which were once praised as the most powerful aircraft in the world. (National Telegram of the 24th)

Philadelphia Former Air Force Chief General Mitchell said in a speech at the Air Defense Joint Conference that the United States is currently threatened by the Japanese air force. Many Japanese aircraft have great speed and can fly long distances. They can fly from Japan to Alaska or the Pacific coast of the United States, drop bombs, and then return to Japan without landing or refueling in the middle. Mitchell also said that the air forces of various countries are developing rapidly, but the United States is stagnant. (Havas Telegram of the 24th)

London Air Defense Exercise Results in Victory for the Attacking Force

Dropped Bombs in Twenty-Nine Places 37

(London) After the British Air Force conducted exercises over London last night, an official from the Ministry of Aviation said today that the attacking force was quite successful.

Three squadrons of bombers, a total of 36 aircraft, attacked the Ministry of Aviation within half an hour after the start of the mock battle, reaching their destination without obstruction. In theory, the attacking force dropped bombs on the Ministry of Aviation from a height of 6,000 feet, and the military supply depot in Kidbrooke was also bombed without resistance. The attacking force made a total of thirty-nine attacks last night, of which thirty-three were indeed blocked, but the attacking force's bombs hit twenty-nine places. (Reuters Telegram of the 24th)

(London) British air defense exercises continued last night, but due to heavy fog, the Ministry of Aviation prohibited all aircraft responsible for defending the capital from departing, in order to avoid unclear visibility and mutual collisions causing accidents. As a result of the exercise, all the targets attacked by the "enemy" aircraft were reached, but the Ministry of Aviation pointed out that the destroyer squadrons responsible for defense did not come out due to the fog, so the attacking aircraft were able to achieve their goals. If a real war were to occur, it would never be like this, so the results of the exercise cannot be considered conclusive. Some people do not regard this exercise as serious. (Havas Telegram of the 25th)

Avoiding Political Topics, the Naval Conference Will Be Difficult to Succeed

Britain, the United States, and Japan Have Not Yet Reached a Compromise Japan Claims There Are No Military Facilities on Mandated Islands 38

(Tokyo) The Foreign Ministry spokesman participated in a press conference held here today, saying that Britain, the United States, and Japan have all agreed not to raise political issues in the future naval conference, especially those concerning East Asia. This decision can be called wise, because if political issues are raised, the conference will fail. (Reuters Telegram of the 25th)

(London) According to news from the Japanese side, Britain, Japan, and the United States have agreed not to discuss political issues at the 1935 naval conference. Political figures here are commenting on this news. According to people closely associated with the government, if political issues are excluded from the naval conference, negotiations are unlikely to succeed. In short, no formal agreement has yet been reached on this point. People here believe that it is best not to involve the political situation of various issues on the agenda of the naval conference. This is in line with what Foreign Minister Simon said in the House of Commons a few days ago, but it is very difficult to avoid certain key points, such as the status of the powers in China and the Singapore naval base, in the naval conference. (Havas Telegram of the 25th)

(Tokyo) The legal effect of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations will take place next March. The Japanese government believes that withdrawal from the League of Nations, whether from a legal or international customary law perspective, has nothing to do with the ownership of the mandated islands. However, it only complies with Article 22 of the League of Nations Covenant, and is obligated to submit an administrative report annually. Last year's annual report was sent to Yokoyama, the Japanese Consul-General in Geneva, yesterday. Furthermore, regarding rumors that Japan is preparing for a Pacific war and has military facilities in the mandated territories, the Japanese government reports the following in accordance with Article 13 of the League of Nations Covenant's military provisions: After the establishment of the South Seas Agency, all temporary naval defenses were withdrawn. Recently, there are no naval deployments or military base facilities on [the] island. There are no military facilities for the islanders either. The maintenance of security in these twelve districts is carried out by the police. (Telegraphic Dispatch of the 25th)

Over the Songhua River

Japanese Fighter Planes Collide, Two Lieutenants Killed 39

(Harbin) The Kwantung Army announced that on the morning of the 24th, the Japanese flying squadron (Captain Tanaka, commander) was conducting aerial shooting exercises over the Songhua River. Two fighter planes operated by Lieutenants Akamatsu and Orikasa of the squadron collided over the Songhua River, ten meters north of Harbin. One sank into the river, and although the other ejected using a parachute, only the aircraft body sank, but both lieutenants are missing. (Telegraphic Dispatch of the 25th)

Polish Warships Visit Russia

Received a Grand Welcome from Soviet Russia A Sign of Friendship between the Two Countries Russian Warships to Visit Poland in October 40

Leningrad The Polish Navy's "Burza" and "Wicher" destroyers, on an official visit to the Soviet Union, arrived in Leningrad today. A grand ceremony was held before the two ships left the Polish naval base of Gdynia to come here. Purtulski, Counselor of the Soviet Embassy in Poland, and Balabanov, Military Attaché, also participated. When the two ships arrived at the sea outside Kronstadt, a Soviet warship greeted them halfway and guided them to the city of Kronstadt. Several Soviet destroyers also guided them here to show respect. When the warships of the two countries arrived at the port of Leningrad (when the flags of the Soviet Union and Poland were flying everywhere), a welcoming guard and naval, land, military, and political leaders came to greet them. On the same day, the Soviet Baltic Fleet Commander Galer hosted a banquet for the Polish guests. Those who attended the banquet included the Polish ship's officers, the commanders of the Soviet Baltic Fleet, and the military and political leaders of Leningrad. During the banquet, Galer gave a speech, saying, "The progress of friendship between the Soviet Union and Poland has established conditions that promote the implementation of friendship between the two countries in economic, political, cultural, and other aspects. The relationship between the military strengths of the two countries has also changed in the same way. I hope that your trip will only be the beginning of the establishment of friendly relations between the navies of the two countries, and will seek a new guarantee for peace in the Baltic Sea." Admiral Enrog, the leader of the Polish fleet, gave a reply, deeply thanking the host for his warm hospitality. Enrog said, "This trip by our warships will be the beginning of forging a closer relationship between the navies of the two countries. When your country's warships visit our country next time, we will thank you for this grand banquet." According to the semi-official newspaper "Polish Daily," Soviet warships will visit the port of Gdynia in October. (TASS Telegram of the 24th)

The National Socialist Party Intends to Disturb Austria, Riots and Bloodshed in Vienna

Rumors that Troops Have Surrounded the Prime Minister's Office and That Dollfuss Has Been Detained 43

(London) Horrifying news from Vienna says that Austrian Prime Minister Dr. Dollfuss and Public Security Minister Fey are being detained in the Prime Minister's Office by members of the National Socialist Party. (Reuters Urgent Telegram of the 25th)

Vienna The National Socialist Party has occupied the Prime Minister's Office, and everyone in the office has been imprisoned, including several cabinet members. Troops are currently surrounding the Prime Minister's Office. The Chief of Police is negotiating with the rioters for the handover of the Prime Minister's Office. It is reported that the Chief of Police of Innsbruck was shot and killed outside the government office by two members of the National Socialist Party. The perpetrators have been arrested. (Reuters Telegram of the 25th)

Vienna The Austrian National Socialist Party today conspired to overthrow the current government by force. The National Socialist Party has had several clashes with the police and the army. Martial law has now been declared throughout the city. The first riot occurred in a large broadcasting station, where the National Socialist Party used the radio station to spread rumors that the Dollfuss cabinet had resigned. The National Socialist Party attempted to occupy Prime Minister Dollfuss's office, but was eventually dispersed by the police and army. (National Telegram of the 25th)

Vienna, Armed riots at the broadcasting station and the Prime Minister's Office have resulted in at least ten deaths in the first two hours. The National Socialist Party attacked the broadcasting station and occupied it before 1:00 PM, immediately spreading rumors that the Dollfuss cabinet had resigned and that President Miklas had accepted Dollfuss's resignation and appointed the ambassador to Italy, Rindlen, to form a new government. As for the reasons for the cabinet's resignation, it was said to be dissatisfaction with the powers of Public Security Minister Fey. By 2:40 PM, the police had expelled the members of the National Socialist Party. Furthermore, according to unconfirmed news, Public Security Minister Fey narrowly escaped assassination. All government agencies are now guarded by national troops with machine guns. (National Telegram of the 25th)

Bern, Switzerland Authorities seized a German motorboat on Lake Constance today, carrying explosives intended to be transported to Austria to carry out terrorist activities. The three crew members were also arrested. It is reported that they are all personnel from the "National Socialist Party Austrian Embassy" in Lindau, Bavaria. The Swiss government has protested to the German government that German ships carrying dangerous goods should not enter Swiss territory without permission. (Reuters Telegram of the 24th)

Vienna, Innsbruck According to news from Innsbruck, Austria and Bavaria, Germany have both increased their defenses on both sides of the border since yesterday. According to news from Salzburg, a large-scale purge has recently been carried out in Bavaria, with many people arrested. (Havas Telegram of the 24th)

A Drama of Seizing the Broadcasting Station 44

Vienna - Today at noon, the broadcasting station announced that the Dollfuss government had resigned and transferred power to Ambassador to Italy, Mr. Lintner. The entire capital was thrown into an uproar. This claim could not be verified. However, it was later heard that there was gunfire from the windows of the Austrian Broadcasting Corporation headquarters. It became clear that there was a reason for the earlier broadcast. The Annagasse building where the broadcasting station was located, and the surrounding streets, were guarded by police carrying rifles. Machine guns were hastily set up opposite the broadcasting station and the Burgtheater. Subsequently, a large detachment of regular army and home guard opened fire on the broadcasting station. The station also returned fire, causing many casualties on both sides. Although a large police force tried to get the public to leave the dangerous area, thousands of people ran to the streets to watch the battle. The government's resignation claim was later formally denied by the authorities.

This afternoon, the police authorities announced a state of high alert. Many people did not believe the broadcasting station's announcement of the government's resignation, thinking it was a prank by members of the National Socialist Party. Upon hearing this news, leaders of the Home Guard and the Army knew something was amiss and quickly mobilized the entire army to surround the station, deploying a tight security cordon to isolate the inner city from the rest of the capital. It was reported that National Socialist terrorists had invaded the broadcasting station. Although they broadcast the false report of the Austrian government's resignation, the station supervisor quickly cut off the power. The remaining staff rushed into the station and captured the invading thugs. Currently, all is peaceful in Vienna. (Reuters, 25th)

Vienna authorities announced that the army had retaken the broadcasting station after a battle with the insurgents. Only eight people invaded the broadcasting station, and all were captured. The station resumed normal operations at 2:45 p.m. (Reuters, 25th)

Key Locations in the Austrian Capital Guarded by Military and Police, National Socialist Party Threatens to Destroy Famous Church 45

Vienna - Today, military and police are stationed at key locations throughout Vienna because the National Socialist Party has threatened that if two National Socialist Party members detained for sabotage work suffer the same fate as the executed socialist Zhe'er yesterday, then National Socialist Party members will bomb the famous St. Stephen's Cathedral in retaliation. The two arrested National Socialist Party members were originally scheduled to be tried today, but at the last minute, the trial was postponed to tomorrow. At the same time, the government announced that the treatment of these two would not be more lenient than that of Zhe'er. St. Stephen's Cathedral is located in the center of Vienna's inner city and was built in 1144, being one of the most beautiful medieval buildings. (Reuters, 25th)

A fierce gunfight occurred at the Reich radio station in Vienna. Someone inside the station fired at the street from the window. The Prime Minister's Office is currently heavily guarded by the Patriotic League. Details are still unknown. (Havas, 25th)

(Vienna) Lin Nai, a member of the Patriotic League in a town near Klagenfurt, was attacked last night when he left home after being summoned by the League headquarters. He was shot three times and died. The identity of the murderer is still unknown. Some people believe that Lin was originally a member of the opposition party and only later joined the Patriotic League, so the murderer may be a socialist. (Havas, 25th)

The German Black Shirt Squad Forms an Independent Organization, High-Level Agencies Exceptionally Active 48

(Berlin) - In view of the merit of the National Socialist Party's Black Shirt Squad in the June 30th purge, German Chancellor Hitler issued an order today elevating the status of the squad to be an independent agency within the National Socialist Party. From now on, he will be directly responsible to the Chancellor and will not have to obey Mr. Lutze. (Reuters, 25th)

Korean Floods 52

Busan - In the two districts of Myeongji-myeon and Daejeo-myeon in Gyeongsangnam-do, the dikes collapsed, and all the rice paddies were destroyed. 25,000 refugees are on the verge of starvation. (Dentsu, 25th)

Seoul - The floods in southern Korea are gradually moving north. On the 24th, the three provinces of Chungcheongnam-do, Chungcheongbuk-do, and Gangwon-do were invaded by floods. The seven provinces south of Seoul were all flooded. In Gyeongsangnam-do, the region was hit by storms again from the night of the 24th. There is no hope of opening the Seoul-Busan line, and it will be difficult to restore it to its former state. As of the 25th, it has been learned that 61 people have drowned, 44 have been injured, 125 are missing, and 3,378 houses have collapsed. (Japanese Union, 25th)

Polish Dike Breach 53

Warsaw - The Vistula River in Sandormierz County south of Warsaw breached its dike today, flooding 1,500 square miles, with an average water depth of about 20 feet. The number of casualties is feared to be very high. Most of the 11,000 residents of the town are now sitting on rooftops, in danger of drowning at any time due to the collapse of their homes, or they will starve to death. The government is currently doing its best to rescue the people of the town. Thousands of soldiers and civilians in Warsaw are working day and night to repair the dike to prevent it from collapsing and causing further flooding. (Reuters, 24th)

London Rainstorm 54

(London) - Today, there was a heavy thunderstorm in England, breaking the long drought. There was torrential rain in London, with water several inches deep in the streets. Some houses were damaged by electric shocks. A fire broke out at Hammersmith Bridge due to a short circuit, but it was extinguished by the fire brigade, preventing a major disaster. Many shops in lower-lying areas were flooded, causing considerable losses. Surface and underground train traffic has mostly stopped, causing great inconvenience to pedestrians. The football field in Leeds is now a vast expanse of water, and the game has been postponed. (Reuters, 24th)

American Heatwave 55

(New York) - The American heatwave has not abated. It is reported that 15 people are dying of heatstroke every hour nationwide. The total number of deaths has now reached 700. The high temperature and duration have broken all previous records. Forests in the Midwest and West have been started by the long drought. Many livestock have died. According to Reuters Chicago, 1,500 workers are on strike at a livestock farm. The situation at the farm is truly appalling. There are 75,000 cattle, mostly transported from drought-stricken areas to Chicago, who have been starving for a long time and are desperate for food, moaning incessantly. Many have collapsed and died in the heat. Today, the temperature reached 104.8 degrees, making it one of the hottest days in Chicago's history. Livestock farm staff are currently doing their best to feed the cattle, but the strikers insist that they will not return to work until their demands are met. (Reuters, 24th)

Page 9

Doumergue's Words Resolve the Dispute, the Undercurrent in France Disappears

Appealing for National Affairs to be Prioritized, Maintaining a Spirit of Unity, Gaining Understanding from All Sides, the Cabinet Remains in its Current State 56

(Paris) - The political crisis is expected to subside due to the intervention of Prime Minister Doumergue. The cabinet will remain in office without changes. This morning, the President separately met with the Radical Party cabinet members and sincerely advised them to prioritize national affairs and not to start party disputes, otherwise the political truce will end. Subsequently, the cabinet held a meeting for two hours and announced that Taittinger's criticism of Chautemps was a personal matter and not an official matter, and declared that the cabinet still maintained that the Committee investigating the Stavisky financial scandal never raised any questions about Chautemps' honor. (Reuters, 24th)

Cabinet Meeting Debate was Quite Fierce 57

(Paris) - The cabinet meeting opened at 5:00 PM to discuss the important issue of the internal conflict between the left and right factions within the cabinet. It ended at 7:00 PM. All cabinet members debated fiercely, but all took national interests as the premise. Prime Minister Doumergue issued a declaration asking them to maintain a spirit of unity. Ministers Herriot and Sarraut first presented the views of the Radical Party. Herriot then expressed his support for Prime Minister Doumergue's proposal to his colleagues. Doumergue's declaration contained many criticisms of Minister Taittinger, and his attitude was extremely moving. Therefore, it was decided to withdraw the Radical Party's request for Taittinger to leave the cabinet and not to discuss it. After the cabinet meeting adjourned, Minister Sarraut recited the declaration issued by Prime Minister Doumergue at the cabinet meeting, which stated that Taittinger's self-defense at the Stavisky fraud investigation committee of the National Assembly was sincere, but this action did not comply with the original restraints of the parties and endangered the existence of the cabinet. But in the current situation, if Taittinger's position in the cabinet is maintained, the Radical Party will not support the cabinet, and the party truce will inevitably be broken. Conversely, if the Prime Minister requests Taittinger to resign, or accepts Taittinger's resignation, the party truce will still be broken, and the Prime Minister himself will be responsible for the breach. Because there are only two ways out at present, either to maintain the status quo or for the entire cabinet to resign. If the cabinet resigns, the Prime Minister himself will no longer be the Prime Minister in the new cabinet. Therefore, Doumergue appealed to all cabinet members to be patriotic and make France secure. Sarraut said that the Prime Minister's appeal has been understood by all parties, so the cabinet will continue to maintain its original state. (Havas, 24th)

The Radical Party's Anger Has Not Yet Subsided 58

(Paris) - After the cabinet meeting adjourned, Radical Party leader Minister Herriot declared that the Radical Party cabinet members would retain their original positions and would not resign, but this incident would be discussed at the Radical Party Congress in October. Also, the presidium of the executive committee of the Radical Socialist Party and the parliamentary group passed a resolution after listening to the explanation of the Radical Party cabinet members, stating that "the presidium of the executive committee of the Radical Socialist Party and the parliamentary group have placed on record the reprimand of Minister Taittinger by Prime Minister Doumergue and endorse the declaration issued by the Radical Party cabinet members after the cabinet meeting." This resolution was released at 11:00 PM, and its wording did not facilitate the existence of the truce cabinet. It can be seen that the current cabinet crisis was saved by Prime Minister Doumergue's sincere advice and his personal prestige, but the anger of the Radical Party has not yet subsided. (Havas, 24th)

Gold Being Transported by Airplane is Stolen Mid-Flight, Suspect Confesses to Throwing it into the Nile River 59

Cairo - A gold bar weighing 25 kilograms and worth 4,000 gold pounds, transported by an Imperial Airways plane from Central Africa, suddenly disappeared, which is very surprising. The gold was transported by land and plane to Heliopolis Airport, and then by car and motorboat to the seaplane parked on the Nile River. This was at 8:30 PM last night. It was transported by Imperial Airways staff and supervised by Egyptian customs officials. At 2:00 AM this morning, two hours before the plane's departure, an Imperial Airways employee found that the gold bar was missing and immediately reported it to the police station. The police station said that the gold bar had been transported to the seaplane and there was no evidence. However, the Imperial Airways management insisted that it had been transported to the plane, but no signed certificate had been obtained. The police station has now detained two suspected employees of the company, one American and one Egyptian, because they were on the plane at a relevant time. Both insisted on their innocence and blamed each other. The police are now searching everywhere and dredging the river around where the plane was parked, but the gold has not been found. (Reuters, 24th)

Cairo - One of the Imperial Airways Armenian employees arrested as a suspect yesterday has reportedly confessed to throwing the gold bar into the Nile River, hoping to retrieve it later. Divers have been searching for it in the river bottom today. (Reuters, 25th)

National Labor Force Statistics 63

(Nanjing) - The 1933 China Labor Yearbook, compiled by the Editorial Committee of the Labor Yearbook of the Ministry of Industry, will be published in early September. According to the editor of the committee, there are 786,716 factory workers in the country, distributed in 2,787 factories in 13 industries. There are 200,743 mine workers, distributed in 45 mining areas. There are a total of 107,480 railway and telecommunications workers. Except for railway and telecommunications workers who are relatively stable, factory and mine workers have experienced a large number of layoffs in 1933. It is estimated that about 120,000 factory workers and 20,410 mine workers were laid off. Thus, the total number of unemployed or jobless people in the country in 1933 is estimated to be over 2.4 million. In addition, more than 20 places such as Korea, Europe, the Americas, and Southeast Asia, the number of unemployed Chinese workers has reached 32,872. (Central News Agency, 25th)

Lunar Eclipse Tonight 67

(Nanjing) - According to the Institute of Astronomy of the Academia Sinica, at 6:54 PM on the 26th, the moon will enter the Earth's shadow and a lunar eclipse will occur. At that time, the moon will still be below the horizon and will not be visible. When the moon rises at 7:03 PM, one-tenth of the lunar surface will already be eclipsed. At 8:15 PM, the portion of the lunar surface obscured by the Earth's shadow will be greatest, reaching 67% of the lunar surface. Afterwards, it will gradually regain its brightness. By 9:36 PM, it will gradually return to its original state. This lunar eclipse will be visible in all parts of China except for Dihua, Xinjiang. (Central News Agency, 25th)

Measures for Tax Exemption on Sunken or Lost Salt 74

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance instructed all salt administration agencies and auditing offices that the practice of tax-free replacement shipments for salt permits lost or damaged due to negligence in various districts is now abolished, and orders to comply have been issued. Repeatedly, merchants from various districts have presented petitions expressing difficulties and appealing for modifications. It is now determined that since the cancellation of replacement shipments for sunken or lost salt has been clearly ordered, there is no reason to suspend its implementation. Regarding merchants transporting salt from production areas to sales locations, they should be instructed to ensure that taxes and fees in the sales districts are covered by insurance, and this should be strictly enforced to fundamentally resolve the issue. However, before the insurance measures are properly planned and implemented, to show consideration for merchants, the following temporary regulations are established: henceforth, all cases of lost or sunken salt permits in various districts, regardless of transport by sail or steam, and whether coarse or refined sea salt, and regardless of the cause of the accident, shall not be granted tax-free replacement shipments, and the field taxes already paid shall not be refunded. Those who have not paid the field taxes or have not paid in full shall be ordered to compensate or make up the difference. However, if the loss is indeed due to a disaster and is reported to the responsible salt administration agency for verification and is not fabricated, then after reporting for verification, the unpaid onshore taxes for the actual amount of salt lost shall be exempted, and the guarantee deposits for pre-paid taxes and salt passing through high-tax areas shall also be refunded according to the actual amount of salt lost. If broken or old ships are used, or salt ships not registered with the salt administration agency are used, or if navigation is negligent or measures are inadequate, resulting in sinking, the onshore taxes shall still be compensated and shall not be exempted. Furthermore, in cases of loss or sinking, the date of reporting must not be more than three days from the date of the accident, and the date of investigation must not be more than three days from the date of reporting, and the date of the investigation report must not be more than five days. If a ship owner fabricates a report of loss or sinking, in addition to ordering the payment of the reported amount of lost salt at the delivered sales price, the ship owner shall be permanently dismissed and prohibited from transporting taxed salt. If a merchant fabricates a report of loss or sinking, it is often the ticket merchant transporting the salt themselves, and the salt ticket shall be cancelled. If the ticket is leased for transport, a fine shall be levied according to the ticket period to serve as a warning. Regarding cases of loss or sinking permits that have already been reported but not approved, and cases of tax-free shipment permits that have already been approved for shipment, since the cancellation has been clearly ordered, there is no need for further discussion. However, to ensure equal treatment, all previous cases where deposits were made shall be exempted from onshore taxes if they were indeed losses due to sinking, to demonstrate fairness. The measures for instructing merchants to obtain insurance shall be properly planned and submitted for approval. (25th Dispatch)

London Naval Preparatory Conference Opens (British Correspondence) 90

Anglo-American Consultation, British-Japanese Mediation, Multilateral Negotiation, Five-Power Opposition

The future of the 1935 Naval Conference is fraught with obstacles, and these obstacles are not easy to eliminate. This is well known to people in Britain and the United States. Therefore, Britain proposed convening a preparatory conference, with Britain and the United States beginning talks in London. At the same time, Japan was invited to join in trilateral consultations, and France and Italy were also invited to participate in multilateral discussions. The Anglo-American talks were held on June 18th at the Prime Minister's residence on Downing Street. The British side was represented by Prime Minister MacDonald, Naval Minister Monsell, Vice Admiral Riddell, and Kellogg, Director of the American Department of the Foreign Office. The American side included Davis, representative to the Disarmament Conference, Bingham, the ambassador to Britain, Rear Admiral Leigh, the counselor to the embassy. They first exchanged views and issued a simple statement opposing Japan's claim to abolish naval ratios and establish equal rights to national defense. Secondly, they also discussed the location of the 1935 Naval Conference, considering London, Paris, or Brussels, but no consensus was reached. That afternoon, Japanese Ambassador to Britain Matsudaira Tsuneo visited British Prime Minister MacDonald at the House of Commons, inquiring about the progress of the Anglo-American consultations and explaining Japan's views. On the 19th, American representative Davis visited the Japanese ambassador to Britain at his residence, explaining the American position and inquiring about Japan's views on naval disarmament. France and Italy have not yet been formally notified. This conference is not very important on the surface, and it does not require immediate conclusions, but the content is still very complex, and there are still many difficulties ahead. For example, whether the understanding between Britain and the United States, the reconciliation between the United States and Japan, and the mediation between France and Italy can be satisfactory, or even whether a temporary peace can be achieved, is questionable. Because naval disarmament at least includes two aspects, one is political issues, and the other is the technical aspects of armaments. If political issues are not adequately resolved, the technical aspects will always be unclear. For example, the biggest outstanding issue in the Pacific Ocean in political terms is the mandate of the Mariana, Caroline, and Marshall Islands. According to the interpretation of international law, since Japan has notified its withdrawal from the League of Nations, if it does not declare its return to the League next year, the mandate should be returned to the League of Nations. However, Japan not only does not indicate that it will return them, but it also builds air force markers, naval bases, and installs various military defenses on those islands, which has caused unease in the United States and attention in Britain. Therefore, technical consultations on naval disarmament will not be easy to reconcile. Moreover, after Japan occupied Manchuria, it had a strong tendency to move south actively, so Britain and the United States are particularly uneasy, and naval reduction is even more difficult. Japan proposed that the preparatory conference should not discuss political issues (leaving aside Manchuria and the three islands north of the equator held under mandate), otherwise Japan would not participate in the conference. The United States is very unhappy with this, while Britain acknowledges it. Therefore, the current talks do not discuss political relations, but focus solely on naval technology.

Even with naval technology, Britain and the United States cannot agree. Britain's coastline is about 70,000 miles or more, and she has colonies all over the world. With colonies come naval ports. It is easy for the British Navy to take on coal, oil, and water. In fact, she does not need giant ships and guns to protect her maritime security and maintain her commercial traffic. However, Britain has a big drawback: it cannot be self-sufficient in food and must rely on overseas supplies, and all her merchant fleets can easily be converted into powerful cruisers. Therefore, she only needs a large number of light cruisers. Britain currently has 50 cruisers, and in two years, 10 will be retired due to old age. Britain plans to build 30 new cruisers, for a total target of 70 new ships. The United States believes that this number is too large and is very detrimental to the future of disarmament. However, the United States must maintain communication between the Pacific and Atlantic Oceans, the security of the Panama Canal, and the effectiveness of the Monroe Doctrine, and therefore must strongly advocate the principle of giant ships and guns, but it cannot openly promote military expansion, so it came up with a way to temporarily maintain the status quo, that is, to extend the Washington and London naval treaties, with battleships and auxiliary ships all in accordance with the previous agreements. This is the difference in opinion between Britain and the United States.

As for Japan, it fundamentally advocates the abolition of the ratio system, claiming that there are new threats from the Vladivostok area and that it wants to maintain peace in the Far East. Britain and the United States agree that this should not be interpreted in this way. The positions established by the three countries are irreconcilable. Moreover, Italy has decided to build two 35,000-ton warships. France believes that Italy's coastline is very short, so why are such huge warships necessary? France and Italy have always been opposed to each other in the Mediterranean, vying for hegemony in North Africa. Now this new problem has arisen, and it will be difficult to resolve at the naval disarmament conference. Britain wants to maintain communication through the Strait of Gibraltar and the Suez Canal, and it cannot help but feel the serious pressure from Italy's expansion of its navy. With such different positions, various divergent claims arise, so how can compromise be sought in the preparatory conference? (June 20th, London)

Hurricanes and Torrential Rains Cause Disaster in Taiwan and Xiamen 100

Three Days of Wind and Rain Result in Significant Losses; Several Feet of Water Flood Zhangzhou City

Xiamen Dispatch: The recent South China Sea hurricane that struck Taiwan and the coastal areas of Fujian, followed by torrential rains, caused Xiamen to experience rain starting on the morning of the 20th. By the 21st, the wind and rain intensified, the day was overcast, and the temperature plummeted from 88 degrees on the 20th to 78 degrees on the 21st, bringing a cool, early autumn-like feel, prompting people to wear lined clothing. On the 22nd, the wind subsided but rain persisted, remaining overcast until the morning of the 23rd, when it finally cleared and the temperature rose to 80 degrees. Taiwan was the hardest hit by the disaster. According to reports from Taiwan, the entire island was enveloped by hurricanes and torrential rains starting on the afternoon of the 19th, with the southern region experiencing the most intense conditions. Various locations were battered by strong winds, causing widespread panic. The island suffered significant losses. The storms lasted three days and two nights, gradually subsiding by the afternoon of the 21st. As of 10:00 AM on the 22nd, preliminary investigations revealed that Tainan Prefecture was the most severely affected, particularly the Beimen, Xinying, and Zengwen districts. Two men died, three people are missing, 111 heads of livestock died, 99 heads were lost, 101 houses were completely destroyed, 71 were half-destroyed, 161 were severely damaged, 264 were slightly damaged, 1,823 households had water reaching the level of the beds, and 11,859 households had water below the level of the beds. 139 non-residential houses were completely destroyed, and 68 were half-destroyed. Furthermore, in the Beigang district, train services were disrupted due to flooding, and 560 houses were flooded. Below Kaohsiung, transportation and communication facilities were damaged by the wind and rain. Although some services had been restored by the 22nd, the situation remains unclear due to incomplete restoration. The extent of the disaster is expected to be severe, with losses amounting to several tens of thousands of yuan. The Gangshan district was the most severely affected, with over 900 households flooded to a depth of six feet. 6,000 residents were forced to seek refuge on second floors or rooftops, enduring the wind and rain in a state of panic for three days and two nights. Relief efforts began on the 21st after the rain stopped, with aid groups providing food to sustain life. Pingtung also sustained considerable damage, with 53 houses flooded. The Jiali district was particularly hard hit, with 150,000 catties of longan pulp and 8,100 tons of bananas damaged. Crop losses in the Taichung Prefecture are also anticipated, with damage estimated to reach tens of thousands of yuan, and 14 houses collapsed. The north-south trunk railway between Zhutian and Gangshan in Taiwan was disrupted due to flooding caused by torrential rains, and service was only restored at 6:30 PM on the 21st. The severity of the disaster in Taiwan is evident.

In Xiamen, due to the hurricane passing through Zhangzhou on the 21st, coastal vessels from Quanzhou turned back, and services were suspended on the 21st and 22nd, only resuming on the 23rd. Only one merchant ship, the Fuzhou, entered the port on the 21st. A Shanghai-bound ship was delayed for three days due to the hurricane and had not arrived as of the evening of the 22nd. A Hong Kong-bound ship entered the port on the 22nd. Inland roads were damaged by the rain, and all Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Xiamen buses were suspended on the 22nd. In Zhangzhou, located downstream of the Jiulong River, and Nanjin, both of which are low-lying areas, heavy rain continued from the afternoon of the 20th to the morning of the 22nd. By the morning of the 22nd, the water level in the river had risen significantly and flooded into the city, including Yanglaozhou and the east and west Malu roads of Xingmin, reaching the height of people's bodies. By 4:00 PM, the river level had risen further, surging into the Minguo Bank on Dingwei South Road, the vicinity of the Yongjing Middle Road to the Taiqingquan Hotel, and the Taigu Bridge, flooding them by several feet. The Xiazaixiang Jiang Normal School for Women and the Shipu community were also flooded, forcing residents to evacuate to upper floors. Many houses and shops placed barriers in front of their doors to block the water, but these were largely ineffective. All roads in Zhangzhou Prefecture remained closed from the 21st to the 22nd due to the flooding. The prices of rice and firewood increased as a result. The price of rice rose from 85 cents per dou to 90 cents per dou, and the price of firewood rose from 47-48 bundles per yuan to 40 bundles per yuan. However, as of the morning of the 23rd, there had been no reports of collapsed houses, and losses were relatively small. Transportation in the surrounding countryside has been disrupted, and the situation remains unclear. (July 23rd)

Tai'an Continues to Crack Down on Fake Military Organizations 101

It is Discovered by Feng Yuxiang's Subordinates that Fake Brigade Commander Zhang Huchen is on the Run

Jinan Dispatch: Recently, disgruntled military personnel have been plotting mischief and organizing fake military organizations in Shandong. The central organization is located in Jinan, falsely claiming to be the Yimin Company, and has appointed several division and brigade commanders to recruit in various counties. A few days ago, Liu Yaoting of the Third Route Army Headquarters' special reconnaissance team discovered and cracked down on the organization in Jinan, capturing several individuals, including the fake First Army Commander, Shu Zhentang, and the First Brigade Commander, Yue Dai, as well as numerous reactionary lists and letters of appointment. The search for remaining members is ongoing. Zhang Huchen, Brigade Commander of the First Brigade of the First Division of the fake military organization, and others were active in the Tai'an area. Yesterday, they were discovered by Feng Yuxiang's subordinates stationed in Mount Tai. After reporting to Feng, Feng ordered his battalion commander, Wang Zhiyi, to work with the Tai'an County Government to crack down on the organization and nip the rebellion in the bud. However, Zhang Huchen had already left, and only one of his accomplices, Song Kunshan, was apprehended. He will be transported to Jinan in the coming days to be jointly tried. The telegram from Tai'an County Magistrate Zhou Baihong is recorded below:

"(Titles abbreviated) I have just received a report from Battalion Commander Wang Zhiyi, sent by Mr. Feng, stating that a fake military reactionary organization has been cracked down in Jinan, and that Brigade Commander Zhang Huchen and others are hiding in the western suburbs of Tai'an. He requested assistance in apprehending them. I immediately dispatched a police chief with officers to assist in the capture. However, Zhang Huchen had already left. We apprehended his accomplice, Zhu Kunshan, who confessed to his knowledge of the situation and admitted to recruiting for the fake army. I have ordered a strict search for Zhang Huchen to continue. I respectfully report this matter, Zhou Baihong, Yang Hai." (July 24th)

Bandits Discovered in Linyi, Shandong Province 102

Bandits Near Nanyang Lake Are Also Active; Han Fuqu Has Dispatched Troops to Search and Suppress Them

Jinan Dispatch: After the clearing campaign in this province, large groups of bandits were largely eliminated. Recently, due to the growing crops, bandits in northern Jiangsu have become active again. According to a report from Liu Huating, Magistrate of Feng County, a group of 50 to 60 bandits from Picheng County, Jiangsu, suddenly crossed into Xujiafangzi, Qingping Township, on the border between Jiangsu's Picheng County and Shandong's Linyi County, on the night of the 21st. The County Magistrate has led local militias and village associations to block and suppress them. After receiving the report, Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu replied by telegram, ordering the County Magistrate to suppress the bandits swiftly and thoroughly, and ordered the Sixtieth Brigade stationed in Zaozhuang to assist.

Furthermore, in the Jinxiang, Yutai, Jiaxiang, Nanyang Lake, and Wenshang areas of southern Shandong, bandit activity has been occurring recently due to the growing crops, disturbing the peace of the region. Residents of the area have jointly submitted a petition to the Provincial Government, requesting the dispatch of troops to search and suppress the bandits and ensure the safety of the people. After receiving the petition, Chairman Han ordered Liu Yaoting, Captain of the Special Reconnaissance Team, to lead a team to search and suppress the bandits and ensure local safety. Upon receiving the order, Liu led 55 officers and scouts, carrying 55 Mauser pistols and 10 rifles, departing at 4:40 PM today (the 23rd) on the No. 1 armored vehicle to search and suppress the bandits.

Furthermore, the Fourth Route Militia of this province, led by Xie Shuxian, was originally stationed in Qufu. Recently, it was transferred to Ju County by provincial order to facilitate bandit suppression yesterday (the 23rd).

Notorious Bandit Wang Yunlong Executed in Southern Fujian 103

Has Terrorized the Huian Area for Over a Decade; Apprehended and Executed by a Detachment of the Governor's Headquarters

Xiamen Dispatch: Wang Yunlong, a notorious bandit in southern Fujian, was executed by firing squad in Zhangzhou on the 20th of this month. Wang, along with Wang Hanmin and his brother Wang Lianmin, were three major bandit leaders in Huian County for over a decade. Their scourge was not limited to Huian County, but extended to Huian, Jinjiang, Putian, and Xianyou. Wang Hanmin was killed in Putian in 1929 by Lin Shouguo, Brigade Commander of the Marine Corps. Wang Lianmin succeeded him as leader of the group, but fled to Shanghai after a defeat. People from Huian reported him to the Shanghai authorities, and he was arrested and executed by firing squad in Shanghai by the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters in 1932. Afterwards, Wang Yunlong commanded the remaining bandits, wreaking havoc in the Huian-Putian area. In 1929, he attacked and captured the Huian County seat, looting the entire city. In addition to these incidents, he engaged in kidnappings, robberies, arson, and murders. Northern Huian suffered the most. When the Central Army entered Fujian to quell the rebellion, Wang also raised the banner of the anti-rebellion people's army. His forces consisted of over 500 men, all armed with modern firearms, including machine guns. Subsequently, the Military Affairs Commission's headquarters issued an order to revoke the title of anti-rebellion people's army and ordered them to garrison in place, awaiting reorganization, and forbidding them from disturbing the people. Wang then entrenched himself in northern Huian, relying on his large number of men and superior weaponry to kidnap and extort in the northern and western Huian areas, engaging in all sorts of illegal activities and leaving Huian in a state of unrest. In March of this year, Song Xilian, commander of the Thirty-sixth Division, stationed troops in Quanzhou, and Li Liangrong, commander of the 216th Brigade, personally led a battalion of troops in five routes to suppress the bandits. Wang suffered a major defeat due to lack of preparation, with over 200 men killed and the rest scattered. Wang fled to Xiamen alone and hid in the house of a foreign national. At the end of April, he was arrested by the Fourth Detachment of the Nanchang Governor's Headquarters stationed in Xiamen. In May, he was taken to Longyan and then transferred to the Zhangzhou Headquarters in June. The Huian Chamber of Commerce, along with various community groups and villages, filed lawsuits against him. The Huian Fellow Villagers Association in Xiamen and the victims listed their grievances and filed lawsuits. The military court opened the trial, and all plaintiffs appeared in court to confront the defendant. After repeated trials, overseas Chinese from Huian also sent telegrams urging that he be brought to justice. The military court requested and obtained case files from the civil affairs department and the Huian County government, conducted a thorough investigation, and sentenced him to death. He was executed by firing squad in Zhangzhou on the morning of June 20th, and his crimes were announced as follows: "Announcement Regarding the Execution of Wang Yunlong, a Notorious Bandit in Southern Fujian, Also Known as Wang Gengmin: It has been determined that Wang Yunlong, also known as Wang Gengmin, previously colluded with his brother, the deceased bandit Wang Hanmin, and terrorized the Tianchuan area of Huian, engaging in widespread kidnapping, robbery, and devastation of nearly the entire county for over a decade, accumulating countless crimes. In June 1929, he attacked and captured the county seat, looting the entire city. In addition, he committed arson and murder. After Wang Hanmin was executed, Wang Yunlong opportunistically joined the anti-rebellion forces, but continued his criminal behavior, entrenching himself in the eastern, western, and northern townships of the county, causing multiple disturbances. Such heinous crimes are unforgivable. Wang has been apprehended and found guilty after a thorough investigation. He has been sentenced to death in accordance with the law. The aforementioned criminal Wang Yunlong, also known as Wang Gengmin, age 30, from Huian County, has been escorted to the execution ground at the foot of Zhishan Mountain today, verified to be the correct person, and executed by firing squad as a warning. This announcement is made, and it includes the execution by firing squad of bandit Wang Yunlong, also known as Wang Gengmin, age 30, from Huian County." (July 23rd)

Guangdong Province Abolishes Likin Taxes and Miscellaneous Levies 104

To Be Implemented from August 1st, with Profits from Sugar Factories Used as Compensation

Guangzhou Dispatch: In recent years, the finances of Guangdong Province have been greatly improved through the streamlining of taxes and the introduction of taxes on imported foreign rice and agricultural products. More recently, the income from the sugar monopoly has further increased government revenue. Therefore, the financial authorities are implementing the plan to abolish the Likin taxes that should be eliminated and to abolish miscellaneous gambling levies in various counties. The losses from these taxes will be compensated for by the profits from the sugar monopoly. Starting next month, the Likin taxes that should be abolished include: the Guangzhou West Tax Office, the Guangzhou East Long Tax Office, the Gaozhou Prefecture Tax Office, the Leizhou Prefecture Tax Office, the Taiping Sanguan Tax Office, the Qiade Tax Office, the Chaozhou Prefecture Tax Office, the Qiongzhou Prefecture Tax Office, the Huangjiang Tax Office, the Foshan Fenshui Xinong Tax Office, the Hua County Luojiang Tax Office, the Yangchun Shanhe Ten Tax Office, the Wenchang Qinglan Yandun Land Tax, the Wenchang Puqian Tashi Land Tax, the Nanxiong Winter Mushroom Grass Mushroom Preserved Duck Levy, the Qiongya Betel Nut Export Levy, the Xijiang Lime Platform Likin, the Qiongya Maritime Defense Fee for the Entire Prefecture, and the Guangzhou Prefecture Tax Office, totaling 19 types. In addition, various miscellaneous gambling levies in 27 counties and cities within the province, such as Fogang, Hua County, Qingyuan, Zhaoqing, Heshan, Gaoming, Yunan, Deqing, Kaiping, Taishan, Jiangmen, Shunde, Shixing, Nanxiong, Yingde, Qujiang, Renhua, Lechang, Luyuan, Lianzhou, Lianshan, Yangshan, Pingyuan, Jiuling, Meixian, Xingning, and Wuhua, will also be abolished from August 1st. The total amount of advance payments made by the contractors for the aforementioned taxes and levies is 220,726 silver dollars, and the contractors for the miscellaneous gambling levies have deposited 277,400 silver dollars, totaling 498,126 silver dollars. These amounts should be refunded by the government. The Department of Finance has already submitted a request to the Provincial Government, which has been approved, to allocate funds from the profits of the sugar factories to refund the contractors in five monthly installments. If the aforementioned Likin taxes and miscellaneous gambling levies are abolished from August 1st, the total loss to the provincial treasury is estimated to be 295,794 silver dollars per month, and 3,549,530 silver dollars per year. The compensation method is to allocate funds from the profits of the sugar factories each month to make up for the loss in revenue, so as not to affect the provincial budget for the 23rd year. The aforementioned plan has already been submitted by the Department of Finance to the Provincial Government for review and approval, and the Provincial Government has issued orders to the Department of Finance and its subordinate departments to comply. (July 20th)

Guangxi Province Implements Business Tax 105

The Business Tax Bureau is Located in Wuzhou, Initially Implementing Business Tax on Pawnshops

Guangzhou Dispatch: In order to streamline finances and increase revenue for the provincial treasury, Guangxi Province has decided to implement a business tax and is actively preparing for its implementation. The Business Tax Bureau has been established in Wuzhou, with Zhang Rui appointed as the Director of the Business Tax Bureau. Starting this month, a business tax will be levied on pawnshops, divided into four grades, with tax rates determined by the amount of operating capital. For example, businesses with capital of 10,000 yuan or more will pay an annual business tax of 200 national currency yuan. Higher taxes will be levied on businesses with more capital. Additionally, a one-time registration fee of 10 yuan and a license fee of 40 yuan will be collected from pawnshops. All regulations regarding the pawnshop business tax have already been promulgated by the Guangxi Provincial Government. The regulations are as follows: Article 1: Merchants and residents operating pawnshops within Guangxi Province, in addition to the regulations stipulated separately for pawnshop operations, shall comply with these regulations regarding taxation matters. Article 2: Whether pawnshop operations are newly established, old, have changed managers, or are inherited from a parent, they shall comply with the regulations stipulated in these regulations and pay the pawnshop business tax. Article 3: Pawnshop operations shall first prepare the full amount of the annual business tax, registration fee, and license fee, and then provide the following information to the relevant county government for verification, collection, and reporting, and then transfer it to the provincial government for registration and filing, and issue a business license. 1. Name, age, place of origin, and address of the manager. 2. Pawnshop name. 3. Business address. 4. Total amount of capital. Article 4: Pawnshop managers who receive a pawnshop business license must have the following qualifications: 1. Be at least 25 years old. 2. Have a solid family background. 3. Have good character and established credit. 4. Have not been declared bankrupt. Article 5: The pawnshop business registration fee is 10 national currency yuan. Article 6: The pawnshop business license fee is 40 national currency yuan per license. Article 7: Pawnshop operations are divided into four grades, A, B, C, and D. The business tax payable shall be collected according to the following capital amounts: 1. Grade A: Capital amount of 50,000 yuan or more, annual tax of 500 national currency yuan (silver dollars). 2. Grade B: Capital amount of 30,000 yuan or more, annual tax of 400 national currency yuan. 3. Grade C: Capital amount of 20,000 yuan or more, annual tax of 300 national currency yuan. 4. Grade D: Capital amount of 10,000 yuan or more, annual tax of 200 national currency yuan. Businesses with capital less than 10,000 yuan are not allowed to operate. The aforementioned tax shall be paid to the relevant county government for verification and transfer within the first month of each accounting year, along with the license fee. Article 8: County governments are allowed to allocate 15% of the pawnshop business tax collected for local expenses, 5% for county government office expenses, and 80% to be remitted to the provincial treasury. Article 9: If the amount of capital reported by the pawnshop is found to be falsely low, once verified or otherwise discovered, a penalty of five times the tax payable shall be imposed. Article 10: 50% of the fines from the previous article shall be retained by the county government as a reward, and 50% shall be remitted to the provincial treasury. Article 11: These regulations shall take effect on July 1, 23rd year. If there are any unaddressed matters, they may be amended at any time. (July 18th)

Anhui Construction Department Carries Out Drought Relief Work 106

Wuhu Dispatch: Since the 18th, the climate in various counties of southern Anhui has changed dramatically, with the average temperature between 84 and 85 degrees Fahrenheit, and the lowest temperature dropping to 78 degrees, a difference of 25 or 26 degrees compared to previous days. There have been several showers each day, but the long period of sunny weather without rain this summer has caused drought in various counties. The most severely affected counties include Shitai, Taiping, Ningguo, Jingde, Qingyang, Jiashan, Jingxian, and Dingyuan. The less severely affected counties include Huaining, Wangjiang, Susong, Guichi, Chuxian, Hefei, Nanling, Quanjiao, Tongcheng, Tianchang, Taihu, Hanshan, Tongling, Lujiang, Fanchang, Langxi, Hexian, Wuwei, Dangtu, Wuhu, and Guangde. Except for Xiuning, Huaiyuan, Shouxian, and Fuyang, which have not experienced drought, it is feared that most of the remaining 26 counties, such as Dongliu, Wuyuan, and Qimen, are also in a severe situation, according to provincial estimates. The Drought Relief Committee organized by the Provincial Construction Department has already carried out the following measures: (1) Ordering county governments to supervise irrigation day and night. (2) Providing detailed instructions on drought-resistant cultivation methods. (3) Conducting a detailed survey of the drought-affected area and crops suitable for the soil. (4) Selecting commonly applicable drought-resistant crop varieties and informing counties to prepare seeds. (5) Installing existing water-lifting machinery near Anqing and inquiring about the prices and types of machinery from manufacturing plants to prepare for procurement. (6) Surveying local grains and formulating follow-up measures to regulate food supplies for the people. (7) Issuing a general order to all counties to supervise and urge people to organize irrigation cooperatives. (8) Issuing a general order to all affiliated agricultural and forestry farms to send personnel to various locations to guide people in diverting water for irrigation and switching to drought-resistant crops. However, the rain has come too late, and the disaster has spread throughout the province. The entire rural economy is likely to be in an unrecoverable state. (July 23rd)

Poor People Seen Seizing Rice in Fengjing, Songjiang 107

Due to the prolonged drought in various ports, the depletion of river water, and the difficulty in transportation, the supply of rice has become scarce, leading to a sudden and drastic increase in rice prices, with differences reaching as much as three or four yuan per stone. The common people struggling to find food are lamenting their plight. On July 20th, at 10:00 AM, Sun Zhengyu of Liezi Weixiang in Fengjing District led more than ten villagers to break into the homes of Xu Zigao, Zhao Fugao, Xu Zitian, Xu Zengrong, You Zengyao, Zhang Hehai, and others in the same village. Claiming that they had no rice to cook and were on the verge of starvation, they took approximately eight stones of rice that was to be used between the spring and winter. The incident was reported by the Village Head, Xu Yuezhou, to the County Government for investigation.

The Enthusiasm of the Suzhou Residents' Festival 108

The Suzhou Residents' Festival is exceptionally enthusiastic and fervent. The ceremonial processions and decorations are becoming increasingly lively. There were two major events on the 24th: (1) The Zhou Wang Festival, with more than 40 types of ceremonial regalia and a participation of 30,000 people. Ancient weapons such as swords, spears, and halberds were displayed, creating a solemn atmosphere. (2) The Mengjiang Festival, with stilt walkers throughout the streets and numerous performances of Heibai Wuchang (Black and White Impermanence), grabbing food, Qian Duxiao praying for rain, Tang Sanzang retrieving scriptures, and the White Snake Legend flooding Jinshan Temple. Humorous performances, gongs, incense flower baskets, and stone locks were also present. The procession stretched for three or four miles. Yesterday (the 25th) also featured two events: (1) The Dongshan Festival, characterized by flags and parasols made of chili peppers, carried by men with pockmarked faces and leprosy, known as the "Pockmarked Lepers," as well as young women and children wearing flower baskets and novel stilt walkers. (2) The Chunshen Jun Festival. Today (the 26th) will feature the Flower King Festival, among others. It is reported that the Bronze Guanyin will be returned to Guangfu on the 31st, and the various temple festivals in the city will continue until the 31st. More events are expected to take place in the coming days.

Strange News of Wool Growing on the Ground in Wuxi 109

Amidst the cries of a prolonged drought, wool has suddenly grown from the cracks in the stone in the Didi Bridge area of Ganlu Xie, Yulin Township, Eighth Autonomous Region of this county. The wool growing from the cracks in the stone on the bridge surface is of various colors, including gray, yellow, and light green, while the wool under the bridge abutment is entirely white. Similar discoveries have also been made in villages near Xiqiao Bridge in Tangkou. It is said that this wool stands upright, root-up, before sunrise in the morning, but falls over after sunrise. The owner of a tea shop in the area has collected wool of various colors and is carefully preserving it for scientific research.

Continued Thunderstorms Reduce the Severity of the Disaster 110

A thunderstorm occurred in the county on the morning of the 24th at 4:00 AM and lasted until 5:30 AM. The average rainfall throughout the county was approximately three inches. The rice fields that have already been planted have standing water, which is expected to last for five to seven days without needing more water. The unplanted fields are only moistened with mud and do not have standing water. Farmers with seedlings are currently using water wheels to transplant the seedlings. Those without seedlings can only lament their fields, or transplant seedlings elsewhere. If the rain continues, the severity of the disaster can be reduced. Since the 24th, the water in the canal has been flowing from east to west, which is due to the higher rainfall in Suzhou compared to Wuxi. This is also a good sign.

County Magistrate Cai of Changzhou Again Requests Resignation 111

County Magistrate Cai Pei of Wuyi County had previously submitted several requests to the provincial authorities for resignation. Local organizations and groups sent telegrams requesting him to remain in his post, which were not approved. Recently, County Magistrate Cai suddenly fell ill and was treated at the Wujin Hospital. He unexpectedly developed a desire to resign again, submitting a request to the provincial authorities to resign and ordering his staff to expedite the handover. According to news from Zhenjiang, the provincial authorities did not approve Cai's resignation but only granted him seven days of leave for recuperation. It is also reported that County Magistrate Cai telegraphed Ye Xiufeng, a member of the provincial government, yesterday (the 24th), requesting him to expedite the approval of his resignation.

Huangtian Port outside the North Gate has not been dredged for many years, and its sedimentation is severe, harming transportation. Previously, Director of Construction Shen came to Cheng to inspect and deemed it necessary to dredge it urgently. The county submitted a plan for dredging to the authorities for approval. Yesterday (the 23rd), the Construction Bureau sent supervising engineer Wang Shixi to Cheng to discuss the method of surveying Huangtian Port with the county government. It was decided to start surveying on the 24th, draw up a map, and submit it to the bureau for approval.

Unemployed Man Commits Suicide at Home by Poison 113

Zhuang Rungui, a resident of Hebei Street outside the East Gate, used to work as a partner at the Qingyang Qinkang Dyeing and Weaving Factory. After the factory closed down, he was unemployed and stayed at home. His wife, Mrs. Zhuang, often scolded him. Elderly Woman from Haimen Dies in Fire 114

Lu Tingzhang, a villager from the northwest of Dahong Town in the Third District, was from a well-off family. The day before yesterday (the 22nd) afternoon, due to carelessness with fire while cooking dinner, a fire broke out. Thick smoke and flames quickly spread. Villagers, alerted by the alarm, rushed to put out the fire, but due to the strong wind at the time, the fire intensified and was not extinguished. All three tile-roofed houses were destroyed. His elderly mother, over sixty years old, was bedridden and unable to escape, tragically perishing in the fire.

Grand Dragon Boat Race in Changshu 115

Due to the lack of rain this summer, a drought was imminent. Many enthusiasts offered sacrifices to the Great White Dragon King to pray for rain for a month, but to no avail. Starting on the 17th of this month, there were occasional showers, especially on the nights of the 21st and 23rd, when the rainfall was the heaviest, totaling about one and a half feet. Consequently, those who had offered sacrifices to the Dragon King attributed the rainfall to its merit and initiated a race. The one at Kuatang Bridge in the city took the lead and held a race on the night of the 24th. The event included various carrying poles, children on horseback, and all kinds of ceremonial guards. The night lights were all made with electricity, shining brightly. As a result, the areas of Siqian Street in the city center, Nanshi Xin, and Xianxi Street were brightly lit with electric lights, creating a huge crowd and an extremely lively scene, which was a grand spectacle for a time, dispersing only at midnight. It is now learned that Huiri Temple in the Central District and the Old Temple in the West City have scheduled races to continue on the 30th and 31st, with even grander ceremonial guards.

Zhenjiang Jiangsu Province Implements Diverting the Huai River into the Sea 116

The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that the route for dredging the river into the sea has already been surveyed by personnel dispatched by the Huai River Diversion Committee. The construction funds of 500,000 yuan have been arranged. It has recently ordered the county magistrates of Huaiyin, Siyang, Shuyang, Suqian, Funing, and six other counties to establish labor conscription offices in their respective counties immediately, conscripting 20,000 laborers per county, with construction starting on October 1st and completed within six months. At the same time, the second phase of the Huai River Diversion project has now commenced and is scheduled to be completed this year. After that, the actual effect of diverting the Huai River to assist transportation can be achieved, and the areas north of the Yangtze River will never have floods, it is said.

Yangzhou Bloodstains Appear on the Ground, Rumors of Dragons Emerge 117

Li Ma, a widow in Miaojin Lane in the city, had five thatched houses. Two of them were rented to Xu Rugen, a barber, his wife, Mrs. Wang, and a rickshaw puller named Ma Deheng. At about 10 PM on the 23rd, Li Ma was cooling off in the courtyard with her granddaughter, Li Xiaofeizi. Suddenly, Li Xiaofeizi cried out that there was blood on her leg. Li Ma immediately examined it and suspected it was a bug bite that caused the bleeding. She wiped it off with a cloth, but when she entered the room, there were multiple spots of blood, which greatly frightened her. She cried out loudly, alarming the neighbors. The crowd suspected the emergence of a dragon and prayed with incense, covering the bloodstains with chamber pots and lime. However, at the time of the screams, Xu Rugen's wife, who was bedridden, heard the sound and cried out to her husband, and he moved out his luggage and belongings together. Seeing that nothing happened, the crowd moved them back. The incident was heard by the Public Security Bureau, which brought Li Ma and others, along with the bloody items, to the bureau for questioning. The bloodstains were sent to the hospital for testing. Due to the bloodstains being dry, they could not be identified. The witnesses have now been sent to the headquarters for handling.

Two Teenagers in Hangzhou Commit Suicide by Poison 118

Sun Hongfang, an apprentice at the Song Yuxing South Goods Store at No. 96 Wangjiang Gate in Hangzhou, had been working at the store for five years with a monthly salary of four yuan. Unexpectedly, he suddenly developed a pessimistic view of life. He secretly bought two ounces of Lysol and swallowed it in secret at night. His colleagues discovered him in the middle of the night and sent him to the hospital for treatment. However, due to severe poisoning, he soon died. Furthermore, a traveler named Feng Jingtian, 22 years old, was staying at the Juying Inn on Huashi Road, in Room No. 66. At midnight, he suddenly swallowed opium to commit suicide. The waiter discovered him and sent him to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. He died at dawn. As no family members claimed the body, the Tongshantang prepared a coffin and encoffined him.

Li Jingzong Goes to Peiping Yesterday 122

Will First Inspect the Lanzhou-Ningxia Air Route and Then Go to Xinjiang to Negotiate with Sheng

The Ministry of Communications once sent personnel to Xinjiang last month to negotiate, but there was still no definite news. Li Jingzong, the general manager of the company, took the 4:05 PM Shanghai-Peiping train yesterday afternoon to inspect Peiping in order to rectify and find ways to remedy the situation. After completing his work, he will conveniently transfer from Peiping to Xinjiang to meet with Sheng again and negotiate, so that Sino-German joint transportation can be realized as soon as possible.

Supporting the Completion of the Ammonium Sulfate Factory 123

Syndicate Provides Huge Low-Interest Loan

Total Loan Amount is 5.5 Million Yuan

Shared and Borne by China and Five Other Banks

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the ammonium sulfate factory is one of the five major basic industries planned to be established by the Ministry of Industry. It was originally planned to be operated with state funding, but due to various obstacles in funding and talent, it could not be realized. It was changed to be established by Fan Xudong, the manager of the Yongli Alkali Manufacturing Company in Tianjin, who raised funds. The fixed capital is 10.05 million yuan, and the Shanghai Syndicate, including China, Jincheng, and five other banks, will lend a low-interest loan of 5.5 million yuan to help it succeed. Now we will explore the details as follows:

Establishing an Ammonium Sulfate Factory 124

Ammonium sulfate is an indispensable raw material in industry. Whether it is military industry, chemical industry, manufacturing industry, or any other industry, it is a necessary product. Especially for agricultural countries, the large amount of fertilizer powder required is of the greatest importance to the national agricultural product yield. There are already more than 100 ammonium sulfate factories in the world, with the most in the United Kingdom, Germany, France, the United States, and Japan. Imports to China are about 16 million yuan per year, which is also a huge loss. The Ministry of Industry planned to invest 15 million from the government to operate this factory, which is entirely state-owned. Later, due to difficulties in raising funds, it was changed to a joint venture between China and foreign countries. As a result, competition for investment from capitalists from the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany was aroused, but it ended in failure due to overly harsh conditions. It was also planned to change it to a joint venture between officials and merchants, but there was still no way to obtain official shares. Finally, it was decided to establish it by Fan Xudong, who has achieved success in operating the Jiuda Crystal Salt Yongda Alkali Manufacturing Company. The Ministry of Industry will provide various conveniences to promote its success. Currently, more than 1,700 acres of factory land have been purchased near Xiejiadian on the riverside in Liuhe County, Pukou. Machines have been ordered from foreign countries, and specialized personnel have been recruited to actively prepare for the project. It is expected that the equipment can be completed within two years.

Total Amount of Equipment Capital 125

Fan's plan is to spend a total of 10.05 million yuan on the equipment for the ammonium sulfate factory. The original capital of Yongli Alkali Manufacturing Company was 2 million yuan. Now, Yongli will be expanded and reorganized,

Adding 3 million yuan of share capital, totaling 5 million yuan, renamed "Yongli Chemical Industry Co., Ltd." The remaining 5.5 million yuan will be borrowed by Fan from China, Shanghai, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Zhejiang Xingye banks. Currently, Zhang Gongquan, the general manager of China, and Wu Yunzhai, the manager of Jincheng, believe that the financial industry has no way out if industry is not developed. Therefore, after several consultations, their opinions have approached, establishing a low-interest, huge loan.

Establishment of Loan Content 126

The total amount of the loan is 5.5 million yuan, with China and Shanghai each providing 1.5 million yuan, Jincheng and Zhongnan jointly providing 1.5 million yuan, and Zhejiang Xingye providing 1 million yuan. This loan has now been fully negotiated and established, and both parties have signed a contract. The content of the contract includes the following items: (1) The entire equipment of the ammonium sulfate factory is mortgaged; (2) Only interest is paid within two years, and the principal is not repaid; (3) Within two years, after the entire factory equipment is completed, 5.5 million yuan of company bonds will be issued, and these bonds will be used to repay the loan banks; (4) The syndicate has not allowed the interest rate to be announced, but according to a certain senior member of the syndicate, the interest rate of this loan is specially reduced to about 6-7% due to the relationship of supporting the development of basic industries. The factory has now ordered machinery from abroad, and the Pukou base is also under active construction. This loan will also be allocated successively as needed by the factory and can be freely withdrawn within the limit.

Shenxin and Other Factories' Ministry-Level Meeting Terminates Reorganization 127

Because the Shareholders of the Factory Believe that There is a Way to Maintain It

Li Shengbo of the Cotton Control Committee Goes to Moganshan to Escape the Summer Heat

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the Shenxin Fuxin Maoxin textile and flour factories operated by Rong Zongjing requested the government to find ways to maintain them due to business reasons. The Cotton Industry Control Committee, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance consulted on the reorganization plan and contacted the Shanghai banking community to borrow money for maintenance. Now that Rong Zongjing has been reinstated, he denies the reorganization.
