Li Shengbo, the executive director of the Cotton Control Committee, has gone to Moganshan to escape the summer heat, it is said.

Shenxin and Other Factories Request Government Relief 128

Due to the Impact of the Global Economic Recession, Rong Re-emerges to Shoulder Responsibility Due to the Rise of Rumors

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the Shenxin Fuxin Maoxin textile and flour factories operated by Chinese industrialist Rong Zongjing, totaling twenty-one, are large in scope and are the only great industry in China. Recently, two sentences ago, Rong's factories were affected by the global economic recession, resulting in inflexible economic turnover and requested government relief. At the same time, Rong Zongjing declared his retirement due to old age and entrusted Wang Yuqing to act as general manager. However, in the past three or four days, Wang suddenly resigned, and Rong made a comeback. The twists and turns in this are extremely varied. A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency visited Rong Zongjing at his head office at No. 421 Jiangxi Road yesterday in order to understand the truth behind this. It happened that Rong had already gone out, so I changed to see an important official of the company, who gave the following conversation:

The request for relief from Shenxin and other factories is entirely due to the impact of the entire global economic recession, so we request the government to provide economic assistance to facilitate turnover. This situation is not unique to China. When large industries in Europe, America, and Japan run aground, the government provides strong assistance or even secretly subsidizes them to prevent collapse. The reason why Shenxin adopted this strategy this time is to imitate this. Taking Shenxin as an example, the special tax paid to the country every day is more than 10,000 yuan, which amounts to more than 3 million yuan per year. After three and a half years, it has paid more than 10 million yuan in national taxes. Other wages, interest, materials, etc. are several times or dozens of times more than this. It cannot be said that there is no major relationship with national strength and people's livelihood. Government relief should also be possible. Therefore, after the presentation was submitted, the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Industry paid great attention to it. The Ministry of Industry drafted a plan for the Executive Yuan to adopt to maintain the national foundation, which is gratifying. However, the plan drafted by the Ministry of Industry abandons relief

and says reorganization and dispatching personnel to investigate and estimate Shenxin's assets. Since the promulgation of the plan, the newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai have competed to publish official news, saying that the candidates for the Shenxin Yarn Factory Reorganization Committee have been determined, and that the committee members investigating Shenxin's assets have completed the estimation of all assets. Recently, there have been rumors that the government is preparing to take over Shenxin and other factories, which is really

horrifying. The Shenxin and other factories have been established for two or three decades and have always been entirely commercial shares. This time, due to the impact of the entire global economic recession, the financing is temporarily sluggish, so we applied to the government for economic relief to maintain business. The focus is on economic relief, and the request is limited to economic relief. However, the Ministry of Industry, without investigation, rashly drafted a plan to reorganize. This move is trespassing on the authority of the Ministry of Finance and abusing its power over Shenxin. In terms of the current situation of the factory, whether it has not yet reached a standstill, there is no reorganization to speak of. Even if it has stagnated, before the original shareholders have agreed, how can there be the possibility of taking it over? Even in terms of the so-called estimation, such as Shenxin No. 9 Factory, which was completed in October last year, has more than 60 acres of factory land in the concession. According to the Public Works Department's valuation, the land price is 25,000 yuan per acre, and the factory building cost 2.2 million yuan. There are currently 80,000 spindles, 15,000 thread spindles, and 500 looms. According to the current cheapest price, it must be more than 8 million yuan. However, this time, after the investigation by the Ministry of Industry and the Cotton Control Committee, they rashly estimated it again, only estimating more than 4 million yuan. Although it cannot be said that there is another purpose for a factory that has only been newly built for a year and is only estimated at half the price, it is difficult to avoid

raising suspicion. For example, for other factories, the purchase price of each spindle must be at least 30 yuan, but now it is estimated at 17 yuan. If it is said that the age of the machine is high, I don't know whether the main parts of the machine body, although old, have been newly configured and are equal to the efficiency of the new machine. Otherwise, Shenxin's number of spindles accounts for one-fourth of the country. I have not heard of much inventory. Moreover, the 80-count fine yarn spun recently has created a new record in China's spinning industry, which also proves that the efficiency of the machinery is not bad. Rong, on the Shenxin side, has a 30-year history of struggle. He has suffered hardships in the past, but he has never sat idly by and watched it collapse. This time, in a crisis, if the government can sincerely help and provide economic assistance, then the future recovery can be predicted. Now, the Ministry of Industry's policy, as evidenced by the official news in the newspapers, has an intention to carve up the industry, so the shareholders of Wuxi Shenxin No. 43 Factory have

a telegram opposing the reorganization. Mr. Zongjing had previously announced his retirement due to old age and weakness, but now, due to the rise of rumors and the increasingly worsening situation, he had no choice but to re-emerge to shoulder the responsibility in response to the extraordinary situation. Therefore, he resolutely resumed his duties on the 20th, and the banking industry has also recently expressed unanimous support to promote this only national industry. In the past few days, the business has had amazing developments. Before the government can provide appropriate relief, Mr. Zongjing is prepared to work hard to maintain the critical situation and prevent the banking industry from being affected, it is said.

Qian Chengxu Reports on the Inspection of Factories in Various Countries 129

China's Industry is Still Better Than Other Countries, It Only Needs to Be Revitalized in Time to Find a Way Out

Qian Chengxu, the executive director of the China Industrial Federation, was dispatched as the employer representative to the International Labor Conference and went to Geneva to participate in the meeting. After the meeting, he was entrusted by various domestic factories to inspect the situation of the industrial circles of various countries and the systems of factory management. Now, Qian sent two communications from Rome, Italy, to the Xinsheng News Agency, reporting on the inspection situation as follows: (1) After a long period of consideration, the scope of inspection has now been finalized and will not be changed. The future report will include two major parts. The first part is the general situation of European and American countries in dealing with social problems. All issues such as social unemployment, labor legislation, reduced working hours, labor exchange, female worker protection, occupational diseases, trade union organizations, and labor savings and insurance are listed in the first part. The second part is the internal organization of factories in various countries. All matters concerning company power distribution, increasing efficiency, worker management, worker distribution, worker welfare, industrial safety, and factory inspection are listed in the second part. Because there are so many famous factories in Europe, it is not allowed in terms of time to inspect them one by one. Now, with the introduction of the League of Nations and a careful selection, it has been decided to inspect one to two factories in one country. In Germany, it is Siemens Electric Company and Zeiss Optical Lens Company; in Italy, it is Fei Ye Tuo Automobile Company; in the Netherlands, it is Philips Electric Bulb Company; in Sweden, it is Sangdai Steel Company; in France, it is Luns Mining Company; in the United Kingdom, it is London Transport Union; in Saar, it is the State-owned Mining Bureau; in the Czech Republic, it is Bajia Shoe Factory; in the United States, it is the American Transport Company. The above-listed locations are a total of ten. Each place is prepared to enter the factory for on-site inspection for six days. It is estimated that the work can be completed within two months. In addition, in various countries, there are also dock warehouse organizations, land and water transportation organizations, agricultural cooperation, production and marketing cooperation, and Denmark's field tax system, etc., all of which have research value, but I have to reluctantly give up because of the limited time and private economy, which I deeply regret. In recent years, Japan's industrial organization has made rapid progress. Its goods have recently reached the South Pacific Islands and even Europe and the United States. The progress of the yarn industry has long overthrown Lancashire in the United Kingdom, making India have to sign an economic agreement with it under conditions to maintain the vitality of the British cotton spinning industry. At this time of extreme global economic recession, the production of various countries is also shrinking, making it difficult to compete with. Investigating in Japan is also a matter of urgency. For this reason, I will spend more time when I return to the country from the UK across the Pacific Ocean to conduct on-site inspections and write a report to tell the people of the country. I have met with many economic experts and important government officials from various countries abroad. Every time I talk about Japan, they all unanimously refer to it as an economic invasion that should be resisted. However, when it comes to its industrial economy, they say that Japan is the only country in Asia with organized and industrialized science. If Chinese industrialists hear this kind of argument, I don't know what they would think. The purpose of my inspection this time is only to collect some materials related to industrial and commercial management in a short period of time and return them to the members of the China Industrial Association to facilitate their current reform of the factory system so that they can learn from it. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Europe and looking around, the degree of the world's economic recession is still evolving in multiplication and division. Almost all kinds of enterprise organizations are showing shrinkage and collapse. It is predicted that China will be in trouble in the future under the general environment, which may lead to a second world war and the evil consequences of re-dividing the East Asian market. For this reason, I had to change my original plan and shift my focus to the current social situation in the world and to study its fundamental diseases. Regarding this section, all of the labor legislation, social unemployment, production distribution, labor organization, etc. of various countries are all within the scope of must-be-inspected. The required labor will inevitably be greater, but Geneva has always been the center for all walks of life in the world to explore social and economic issues. The collection of materials and the guidance of experts can all be adequately supplied and assisted. I only spent ten days here, and the details and outlines of what should be inspected have been largely determined. In the future, traveling to various countries, following the map to find the way, will not take much time, and I deeply believe that the future report will reach the country and will be suitable for China's situation and give general readers satisfaction.

Each country is superior. Because China is not originally an industrial country, it has various social and economic conditions. What is considered necessary in industrial countries is not felt to be needed in the country. Therefore, the impact of the world's economic recession is the latest. Even in terms of the current situation, there is still room for maneuver and resistance for a considerable period. As for Europe, its golden age has passed. From July 1933 to the present, the number of productions in various countries has actually decreased to more than 30% on average in surveys that cannot be published. The average discount on all accumulated commodities is also below half, so they all have to adopt a high tariff policy to maintain their own destiny. Recently, the British House of Commons put forward a bill advocating to further increase tariffs on imported goods to the extent that it is sufficient to protect domestic industry. At the same time, the German Minister of Finance also issued a declaration to stop purchasing foreign raw materials. In addition, in the British and Dutch South Pacific territories, tariffs on Japan will be increased separately to prevent dumping. All these kinds of situations are enough to show that the economies of various countries in the world are in extreme panic. I don't know what the situation will be after 1935. Our country has always been a self-sufficient country. As long as we revitalize in time, we may be able to find a way out in this harsh global environment, which is not impossible in fact.

Holders of 96 Public Bonds Telegraph the Ministry of Finance Requesting Reorganization 132

Ministry of Finance replies with disapproval

The 申時社 (Shen Shi News Agency) reports that there were rumors last month about the reorganization of the 96 public bonds, which briefly pushed the price above the 20 yuan mark. These public bonds were issued by the old Northern Government, so most of the bondholders are in the North. They have been inquiring with the 銀綫業公會 (Silver Thread Industry Association) about the reorganization plan. The 銀錢業公會 (Silver Money Industry Association), based on the declaration of bondholders after the January 28th Incident, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance. The Ministry of Finance replied that due to various irregularities during the issuance of the 96 bonds, it is difficult to reorganize them at this time. The declaration of the bondholders is only a unilateral hope and cannot be used as a basis for approval. The local banking community has received telegrams between the Beijing 銀錢業 (Silver Money Industry) and the Ministry of Finance, indicating that reorganization is still a long way off. The 申時社 (Shen Shi News Agency) reporter has transcribed the original text as follows: The Beijing 銀錢業公會 (Silver Money Industry Association) telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance, we have investigated that the 96 bonds and the two reorganized bonds were almost entirely purchased by Northern merchants and civilians during their issuance. Although a small number have been transferred to Shanghai, the majority remains in the North. For more than ten years, the principal and interest have not been paid, and reorganization has been unheard of. The Northern people and businesses holding these bonds are in dire straits, like those drowning or on fire, and the situation has long been known to your Ministry. Recently, the Minister visited 平 (Ping) to investigate business conditions, and the 平 (Ping) citizens and the public eagerly hope for reorganization. These two bonds would rescue the Northern market, like waiting for rain during a severe drought. Therefore, they inquire with the association about this matter daily, and those who bitterly recount their hardships number dozens each day. Therefore, our association convened a general meeting, and it was stated that after the Shanghai Incident in February of the 21st year of the Republic (1932), the prices of government bonds plummeted. The 96 bonds and the two reorganized bonds were similarly affected. At that time, the bondholders negotiated with the government to extend the repayment period and reduce the interest rates of various bonds, and there were 14 articles of reorganization of the principal and interest of the 96 bonds and the two reorganized bonds. The bondholders issued a declaration, and the government issued a clear order and your Ministry issued a proclamation, each with a record. Since that declaration, your Ministry has never been late in repaying the principal and interest of various bonds, demonstrating great credibility, which is admired by the whole country. However, upon investigating Article 14 of the declaration of bondholders, it states that the Ministry of Finance should allocate funds within three years to repay the principal and interest of the 96 bonds and the two reorganized bonds, and the method will be determined by the Ministry of Finance. Now, two and a half years have passed, and no preparations have been made. The number of Northern civilians holding these two types of bonds is very large. They urgently hope to implement the aforementioned declaration, reorganize these two bonds, so that the market can circulate, which is urgently needed for the local situation. Our association immediately unanimously decided to appeal on their behalf and respectfully telegraphed your Ministry for review and approval. We hope that your Ministry will consider that these two types of bonds are of great importance to the Northern people and market and approve the maintenance of the previous plan, promptly plan the reorganization method to relieve the people's difficulties, which is both a public and private virtue." The Ministry of Finance replied, stating: "The Beijing 銀錢業 (Silver Money Industry) Association, we have read your telegram. The amount of the 96 bonds and the two reorganized bonds issued by the old government in Beijing was unlimited, the use of the funds is difficult to verify, and the guarantee fund was not clearly designated. It is difficult for our Ministry to handle. When the interest rates and repayment periods of various bonds were reduced during the previous consultation, although the representatives of the bondholder association proposed reorganization, there were many difficulties in reality. The declaration of the bondholder association regarding internal debt is only a hope of the bondholders themselves, and our Ministry has no approved plan. Currently, the treasury reserves are extremely strained, making it impossible to handle. Please be informed." (Seal of the Ministry of Finance)

Wu Zhihui's Letter to Chen Gongbo 133

Regarding the Reorganization of the Shen Xin Factory

The 新新社 (Xin Xin News Agency) reports that the reorganization of the Shen Xin, Fu Xin, and Mao Xin textile and flour mills has been formally denied by Rong Zongjing, the founder and current general manager of these factories. We have learned that Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, recently sent a letter to Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry, in which he made poignant and humorous statements about the actual situation of the Shen Xin factories and the reorganization. The 新新社 (Xin Xin News Agency) reporter has found the original text as follows: "To Mr. Gongbo, I am pleased to hear that you have been working tirelessly day and night for the safety of the early Xin. I am extremely impressed. The plan for creditors and government representation that you have presented, which is based on scientific methods, is naturally the right path, and I would not dare to add anything further. However, I have something to contribute to dispel the creditors' fear of the saying you heard from the creditors, 'It is not difficult to maintain, but the biggest fear is restoration.' I can further explain the core of what I said in my previous letter. The 'core' I mentioned in my previous letter does not refer to the position of Mr. Rong personally. When I used this phrase in the case, I was afraid of creating a problem with the wording, so I added a clarification at the end of the letter, stating that 'The 'core' mentioned in the letter does not refer to the recent changes in nominal managers, etc. These are internal routine matters that can be changed as appropriate.' Therefore, regarding what you heard the creditors say, 'Taking Mr. Rong as the center, I am afraid of repeating the mistakes of lack of organization and management,' I absolutely do not mean to take Mr. Rong as the center. I believe that regardless of who is taken as the center, if there is a lack of organization and management, the same mistakes will inevitably be repeated. Moreover, the Rong mentioned, or perhaps the Shen Xin becoming the private property of an individual surname, I am convinced that Mr. Rong does not have this intention, at least I am convinced that Mr. Rong Zongjing personally does not have this intention. The reason for my conviction is based on my own theory. Throughout my life, I most admire Chinese individuals, but I do not want China's future to be like them, namely wealthy individuals who maintain their fortunes and quickly pack up their old businesses that have reached millions, saying that if they can do this, it is enough, and knowing when to stop can avoid danger. In the past twenty years, influenced by the West, some have expanded to tens of millions while maintaining their fortunes, but these are all rich people, not new-style entrepreneurs. China cannot compete with the world in commercial warfare because of this. The distinction between wealthy people and entrepreneurs is the big question of whether capitalists should be immediately overthrown. Wealthy people-style capitalists should undoubtedly be immediately overthrown, or at least overthrown soon. The Premier did not want to abolish capitalists abruptly, referring to the capitalists who are entrepreneurs, who are actually a transitional product of evolution, and not only should they not be immediately overthrown, but they should also be relatively encouraged. There is another type of person that I want China's future to emulate, but I personally have doubts day and night, and I dare not associate with them and have decided not to emulate them. I laugh at myself for only being given a sesame seed-sized piece of courage by Yan Luo Wang (King of Hell), while millions and tens of millions of people

Maintain Their Fortunes 134

Even Yan Luo Wang (King of Hell) does not allow them to dream of it. This person I do not want to emulate is a daring and enterprising figure. I believe that daring and enterprising figures are actually unscrupulous profiteers. The distinction between them cannot be made with precision, and even children can know it in their hearts even if they cannot say it. That is, whether the person fundamentally has a fraudulent mind is obvious, and cannot be concealed in the end. However, I am too lazy to distinguish, because there are unscrupulous profiteers all over China, so according to my nature, whenever I encounter someone who is slightly skilled and temporarily successful, I think they are just having good luck, and the end is coming. I measure them in this way, but sometimes I ask myself if it is too unreasonable to dismiss them all like this, so I also observe them from time to time, and I feel that they fundamentally do not have a fraudulent mind, and I feel that their ability to achieve great success is due to their unique talent for taking risks. I believe that Mr. Rong personally has a talent for taking risks. From a business perspective, putting such people on the battlefield of world commercial warfare makes them valuable figures, and maintaining their fortunes may not be their strength. They are entrepreneurs. In this era of commercial warfare, China can either choose not to join the commercial war, or if it knows that there is no hope for domestic products to stand on their own without participating in the commercial war, then a wise society should protect such figures, and a wise government should especially protect them. That is, even without adhering to maintaining their position, they should also protect their personality and their spirit. The 'core' that I mentioned that cannot be lost is the spirit of Mr. Rong's talent for taking risks. You also heard people say, 'Mr. Rong has only been issuing empty checks in recent times,' and you think that Mr. Rong is close to unscrupulous profiteering, which raises a question about his personality. This person is inevitably very wrong. This is the responsibility of society, and especially the responsibility of the government. All countries help such enterprising figures through society and the government, so that checks do not end up being empty checks. Who actually has a gold mine or silver mine with thirty miles of surrounding land passed down from their ancestors to be entrepreneurs from the beginning? Therefore, the saying 'The biggest fear is restoration' is only a lighthearted expression of humor. Once it is heavily relayed by others, it can turn Mr. Rong into something that is truly unacceptable, and rewards and punishments become unclear, which inevitably discourages heroes. In terms of ordinary Chinese individuals, who would not want to own a few million, maintain their fortunes, and be a wealthy person for life, going to the mountains to escape the heat in this sweltering weather and enjoy their remaining years? Who would want one factory or two factories, even ten factories or eight factories without end, and still

Eagerly Advance 135

This is really driven by a spirit of adventure, and it is definitely not just the obsession of the God of Wealth. It must be known that the God of Wealth is the most stingy and is unwilling to obsess people with shocking numbers. He gives a little, and if they do not maintain their fortunes, he will take it away. Therefore, the creditors' so-called 'Wait until the debts are cleared, and then return everything to Mr. Rong, which is the intention of honoring virtue and repaying merit,' is like the clay bodhisattva in the God of Wealth temple, who often has this temper. It is definitely not appropriate in today's world where countries are standing side by side in a commercial death struggle. According to my ideal, both sides will lose. The first loss is that there is a great intention to clear the debts and disband immediately, as if being bitten by a white dog, they should be afraid of even seeing a white sheep. Creditors do not dare to lend money, and even American banks did not believe it the year before last and learned from us by opening a secret vault to store cash. This is the root cause of the worldwide economic downturn in recent years, so Roosevelt resolutely intervened, and the American financial community also made relative corrections. Our government should not support this passive approach. Another loss is that after working hard to pay off Mr. Rong's debts, they take a large sum of money to honor merit and repay virtue, persuading him to maintain his fortune from now on and open a vault for storage, purely turning Mr. Rong into a wealthy person. Our government would be no different from overthrowing entrepreneurs to reward wealthy people, which is not justifiable. What is called the commercial world, what is called finance? We outsiders firmly believe that it is lending money, managing businesses, and using credit to circulate in the market. Lending only to wealthy people and not to entrepreneurs is a passive commercial world, a rigid finance, with no fighting power, and further, it is a state of economic downturn. Lending absolutely recklessly and randomly is naturally unreasonable, but those who manage businesses should hope that they are entrepreneurs, and those who lend money should also hope that they are entrepreneurs. If they cannot see clearly with their eyes and cannot open their hands, there is no talent for taking risks, and there are not many people who can be called entrepreneurs now. If a person has virtue to honor and merit to repay, and the person has shortcomings, they must have strengths. Is it not worth cherishing heroes and using scientific methods to remedy their shortcomings and use their strengths to pull businesses along with entrepreneurs, creating a positive commercial world? My blind thoughts are not completely worthless, so why should everyone pack up and make people work hard,

Pay Off Debts 136

And repay people, take the remaining money, and enjoy themselves? What I said in my previous letter, 'I am afraid that it will be regarded as ordinary commercial gains and losses, or biased towards passive maintenance. If the core is lost and foreign forces destroy it, who knows that it will not shrink from passivity and eventually collapse,' is because I knew this would happen. However, these passive methods are formed because of 'The biggest fear is restoration.' Why fear restoration? Because of 'Fear of taking Mr. Rong as the center and repeating the mistakes of lack of organization and management.' Lack of organization and management, and the same mistakes have been repeated, is naturally something that is unacceptable, and this restoration naturally cannot be allowed to happen again. If it has not been repeated, and if this failure is considered a repetition, it would be too wrong to wrong Mr. Rong in this way. Not only was the old organization and old management not relaxed, but the application was based on his heart, and some small tricks and details must still be worth retaining if experts carefully study them and improve them to suit the Chinese situation. Shanghai County Government's Drought Relief Measures 139

Extracting Five Measures

The Shanghai County Government, considering that the weather has been dry since the beginning of summer, affecting the livelihood of the people, urgently sought to provide relief. Therefore, it formulated drought relief implementation measures. On the one hand, it prepared a letter and sent personnel to the Provincial Agricultural Implement Manufacturing Factory to negotiate the rental of water pumps, which would be distributed to various districts for subletting and application. On the other hand, it printed and distributed the measures to various districts, instructing the township chiefs to implement them earnestly. Now, the measures are extracted as follows: (1) If the water pumps are insufficient, the rice milling machines will be ordered to be converted into water pumps. (2) If there are surplus manual or animal-powered waterwheels prepared by the people in this county, the district will collect them and lend them to other places in need. (3) If the manual waterwheels in each district are insufficient, the district and township offices will investigate and persuade wealthy farmers to purchase additional ones. (4) Farmers who are unable to afford the cost of digging wells, building dams to store water, and purchasing waterwheels can apply for loans from rural credit funds. (5) For agricultural plants that cannot be sown due to drought or that have withered due to lack of irrigation, the public will be persuaded to quickly change to drought-resistant plants.

The Japanese Textile Manufacturers Association in China Requests Reduction of Cotton Import Tax 141

Chairman Funatsu Seeks Opinions from Chinese Yarn Merchants; Minister Kong Explains in Detail the Cotton Tax Increase

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, after the implementation of the new import taxes in our country, the Japanese Textile Manufacturers Association in China, led by Chairman Funatsu Tatsujiro, has not only requested a reduction in cotton import taxes but also visited Minister Kong to solicit opinions from leaders in our textile industry. Details are as follows:

Please Restore the Old Tax Rate: The association requests the Ministry of Finance to reduce the cotton import tax rate and restore the old tax rate, citing the following reasons: (1) Increasing cotton import tariffs will effectively block exports, leading to an oversupply of products, a drop in market prices, and ultimately the decline of the cotton industry. As a result, cotton farming will be negatively affected. (A) Currently, the cotton yarn and fabric industry in the Republic of China, although forced to shorten working hours to a certain extent due to the weakened purchasing power of the people, is still inevitably facing an oversupply. Therefore, it relies entirely on actively promoting the export of surplus products to maintain the balance between supply and demand. However, the cotton products of competing countries in the destinations of these exports use tax-free raw materials, making competition extremely difficult. (B) The cotton import tax initially started at only six jiao of silver per dan, then increased to one tael and two qian. By May of last year, it had further increased to 3.50 customs taels of silver per 100 kilograms, which meant a tax of about 17 yuan per bale of cotton yarn. This time, it has been further increased to 5.00 customs taels of silver per 100 kilograms, which means a tax of 24 yuan per bale of cotton yarn. This is about six to seven times the initial tax rate. Imposing such a heavy tax will inevitably lead to the cessation of product exports. (C) If cotton product exports cease, the result will be trade deterioration externally and the wasteful dumping of surplus products internally, along with fierce competition among spinning mills. This will inevitably lead to an expansion of the scope of shortened working hours or the forced closure of factories, increasing the number of unemployed workers. Consequently, cotton consumption will decrease, leading to a drop in cotton market prices, which will not benefit the rural areas or help encourage cotton planting. (2) Increasing import tariffs on raw cotton will increase the burden on domestic consumer classes. (A) The average annual import volume of foreign cotton into China over the past five years is approximately 3.27 million dan. Due to climate and soil conditions, most of these foreign cotton species are not suitable for cultivation in China. To achieve self-sufficiency, it will take many years. Therefore, suddenly increasing tariffs today and providing protection cannot be expected to rapidly increase production. (B) Today, rural infrastructure has not yet been implemented, and its effects are not yet visible. A sudden increase in tariffs will not prevent the import of these special raw cotton varieties, but will only increase the tax burden on domestic consumer classes, reducing their purchasing power.

Minister Kong's Explanation: Funatsu Tatsujiro, Chairman of the Japanese Textile Manufacturers Association in China,

believes that the increase in cotton import taxes after the implementation of the new import tariff regulations in our country has a significant impact on Japanese textile factories in China. He sought the opinions of leaders in our country's yarn industry, such as Nie Lusheng, on the increase in cotton import taxes in his private capacity. On Thursday of the previous week, he visited Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi at the Central Bank on the Bund to state the reasons for requesting the revocation of the new cotton import tax policy. Minister Kong explained in detail that the purpose of increasing cotton import taxes this time is to help our country's rural areas and encourage cotton farmers. At the same time, customs revenue will increase. As for the reduction of taxes on cotton textiles and paper, they have been carefully reviewed repeatedly. Therefore, he does not agree to reduce the cotton import tax.

Funatsu's Remarks: A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency visited Funatsu Tatsujiro, Chairman of the Japanese Textile Manufacturers Association in China, yesterday morning. According to him, the reasons for the association's request to reduce cotton import taxes have been detailed to the Ministry of Finance. Minister Kong's opinions on the tax increase are well-reasoned, but in fact, the workers employed by Japanese textile mills in China are all Chinese, making them no different from Chinese factories. Only the capital belongs to Japanese merchants. China's annual exports of cotton yarn and cloth, such as 541,000 dan of cotton yarn and 288,000 dan of cloth heads last year, are all produced by Japanese yarn mills and Chinese yarn mills in China. After the raw cotton tax increases, it will be impossible to promote these exports abroad and instead promote them domestically, which will intensify the business competition between Chinese yarn mills and Japanese yarn mills. In the future, both Chinese and Japanese yarn mills will suffer significant losses.

Shanghai-Tianjin Shipping Merchants Held a Meeting Yesterday 142

Signed a Shipping Cooperation Agreement

After a two-week trial run of cooperation between Shanghai and Tianjin shipping merchants, which began on the 18th of last month, it was decided to continue due to the good results. The participants include the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and 21 private companies: Sanbei, Zhengji, Yuda, Zhidong, Haichang, Beifang, Zhaoxing, Datongxing, Huitong, Yong'an, Tianjin, Zhongtai, Hefeng, Huatong, Funing, Shun'an, Shenquan, Shou Kang, Yuanxing, Huaning, etc. They signed the Shanghai-Tianjin Shipping Cooperation Agreement the day before yesterday. However, the participation of British companies Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire is based on an agreement signed with the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which is responsible for handling it.

Establishment of a Joint Association: The participating shipping companies have established the Shanghai-Tianjin Shipping Joint Association, dedicated to handling cooperation matters. The location is inside the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association on Guangdong Road. A joint meeting was held yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM to establish the joint association. The committee members were nominated by each shipping company, one person per company. All participating shipping companies are required not to violate the agreement. Each member must deposit a guarantee of 2,000 yuan with the joint association, which will be transferred to the bank to earn interest.

Priority for Grain: The cooperation agreement stipulates that priority is given to rice and flour because the transportation of rice and flour from Shanghai to Tianjin is the largest volume. The freight rate and commission are unified. The price charged by each shipping company must be listed with the name of the goods on the manifest after export and sent to the joint association to be forwarded to all shipping companies that have joined the agreement. The freight rates for other goods will be gradually processed.

Fruit Vendors in the Concession Gathered Yesterday to Implement Disruption 144

Melons and Fruits Scattered in Front of Goods Stores in Various Places

The Trade Association Admonishes Strict Adherence to Order

Fruit peddlers in the Shanghai International Settlement area, due to the overly strict crackdown by the police, have found it difficult to make a living. Several hundred of them gathered a few days ago to petition the Chamber of Commerce and the Citizens' Association and held a meeting at the Chinese Public Garden, which was dispersed by the authorities, resulting in no outcome. After deliberation yesterday, several hundred peddlers were assigned to groups and went to the vicinity of goods stores in various places such as the Sixteen Pontoons, the Old Zha Gate Bridge, and the New Zha Gate Bridge to destroy melons. The details are as follows:

Implementing Disruption: Peddlers in the Shanghai International Settlement area have always been selling along the roads, but they are of mixed quality, so some peddlers are disliked. The Second District Citizens' Association requested the Municipal Council to stop them. The Municipal Council agreed to the request and sent police vehicles to arrest and punish them at any time, sometimes three or four times in one place. Therefore, it is difficult to make a living and maintain a livelihood. Several hundred peddlers gathered a few days ago to petition the Chamber of Commerce and the Citizens' Association. Because there was no satisfactory result, it was decided by the general meeting to carry out disruptive actions in the vicinity of goods stores. If a customer buys watermelons or various fresh fruits, they will be attacked as soon as they leave the store, resulting in a mess on the ground, beyond repair. They scatter in all directions, and the buyers can only shout helplessly.

Unable to Sell: Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, these peddlers were disrupting business in the South City Sixteen Pontoons, the North City Old Zha Gate Bridge, the New Zha Gate Bridge, and the Hongkou Wusong Road, forcibly preventing buying and selling. Goods stores in various places reported to the police to send police to stop them because it concerned the entire business. But they came and went without being caught, so the melons were all stored in the stores, unable to be sold. The villagers were very frustrated because the melons they carried could not be stored for long in the hot weather, and if they were stored for a long time, they would rot.

Trade Association Opinion: According to the person in charge of the local Goods Trade Association, the members of the association reported to the association this morning (the 25th) that fruit peddlers in the Shanghai International Settlement area have been forced to stop business because they are unable to make a living due to the strict crackdown by the authorities. Many peddlers have been assigned to wait on the roads near the stores, prohibiting other peddlers from buying goods and doing business from the stores. After investigation by the association, it is confirmed that this is true, and attempts have been made to persuade them, but it is difficult to avoid. However, if the authorities do not resolve this dispute immediately, it is feared that it will expand further and become difficult to manage. In the association's opinion, it should be discussed from two aspects. For the peddlers, in order to maintain their livelihoods, they must ask the authorities to handle the matter leniently. This negotiation should be organized and must strictly adhere to order, without hindering public security. It is not appropriate to use coercive means to prohibit other peddlers from doing business. If this is done, although it is out of anger, it is actually a criminal act. In reason, several representatives should be elected to petition the authorities, requesting that the usual practice be maintained so that peddlers can make a living, or ask local citizen groups for assistance. Furthermore, it is not appropriate for the peddlers to stop business because of this, because if the peddlers do not do business for one day, they will not be able to live for one day. They should continue to do business and temporarily try to avoid the crackdown by the authorities while negotiating. A considerable solution can be obtained. For the authorities, they should take into account the livelihood of the general small-business citizens and cannot only consider administrative measures. They should know that the peddlers are all forced to enter the city due to social and economic difficulties and rural bankruptcy, unable to make a living in their hometowns, and make small profits by selling small items to support the lives of several family members. Therefore, the authorities should take both sides into account when cracking down on peddlers within the settlement and handle the matter flexibly and leniently. Then this dispute can be eliminated invisibly. Otherwise, if it is not resolved for a long time, it may hinder local security.

The Municipal Council Considers the Safety of Pedestrians on the Road 148

Inquiring About Everything from Police Departments in Various Cities in the United States

Please, the Police Department, Pay Close Attention to the Safety of Pedestrians

A director of the Municipal Council recently made two suggestions regarding the safety of pedestrians on the road: one is to widely publicize the dangers of crossing the road and wandering on the road in important places, and the other is to establish safe zones for pedestrians to cross the street, similar to other cities. This proposal was submitted to the Traffic Committee for discussion. According to the report of the Chief of Police, most of the people injured in road accidents are illiterate, so the effectiveness of danger warning signs is doubtful. Also, not many accidents occur at intersections, but more occur because pedestrians rush across in front of fast-moving vehicles. Currently, the guidance on paying attention to danger is provided by public storytellers who explain to the public, and most important intersections have yellow parallel lines for pedestrians to pass. But in fact, very few people use them. As for setting up safe pedestrian platforms on the road, it is difficult to do because the roads are not wide and there are tram tracks on Nanjing Road and Jing'an Temple Road. A committee member said that in the northern United States, they tried to implement a method that required pedestrians to cross the street at designated locations and obey the instructions of traffic police, but the public was unwilling to cooperate, resulting in no effect. The traffic problem in Shanghai is even more complicated, and piecemeal reforms are impossible without thorough and careful study. For reference, the police departments in various cities in the United States can be asked about their classification and analysis methods for road accidents. After discussion, it was agreed that the safety of pedestrians is becoming increasingly important and that the Police Department should pay more attention to it at any time.

Sand Barge Wrecked by Hurricane 152

Gongyuanfa Copper Sand Suffers Disaster; Crew Members Fall into the Sea; Ship Collides; Haizhou Rescues and Sends to Shanghai

The Gongyuanfa sand barge, owned by Yishengyong in Qingdao, has been sailing to ports such as Yingkou, Dalian, and Andong, carrying passengers and goods. After unloading goods in Dalian this time, the ship was instructed to sail to Qingdao to load northern goods, grains, etc. valued at over 50,000 yuan. It sailed to Shanghai, and on the 17th of this month, after loading the goods, the shipowner, Mr. Wei, was ordered to set sail immediately. On the 21st, while sailing on the Copper Sand waters, it suddenly encountered a hurricane. The deck was struck by wind and waves, and three crew members working on the ship were swept into the sea. Wei and the crew were extremely alarmed and immediately lowered the sails. However, the wind was strong and the waves were high, and the ship was tossing and turning. They had no choice but to go with the wind. Unexpectedly, a huge gust of wind broke the main mast. At this point, the entire crew was even more panicked and cried for help. No ship passed by. Later, the ship was hit by waves and collided with the foot of the mountain at the north entrance of Copper Sand. The ship broke apart. When it ran aground, several more crew members fell off the ship. The ship immediately sounded the gong for help. Until dawn, a ship from Haizhou passed by and lowered its gangway, sailing to the foot of the mountain and rescuing the crew members to the ship. The ship then transported them to Haimen, where the ship's staff pooled 20 yuan and gave it to the shipowner, Wei. Yesterday, Wei and the rescued crew members took a ship to Shanghai and reported to the goods consignees. He also telegraphed the Qingdao consignees. It is said that there were a total of 31 people on the ship. Eighteen people have been rescued and arrived in Shanghai. Thirteen people were swept away by the wind and waves during the disaster. In the chaos at the time, it was difficult to take care of everyone. Although the ship ran aground at the foot of the mountain and the bottom and sides of the ship were broken, the inside of the ship was flooded. It is unknown whether the ship's cargo can be towed out of danger. The cargo consignees must go and inspect.

A Rotting Male Corpse Floats in the Suzhou Creek 153

Suspected to Be a Man Who Planted Lotus Flowers After Being Assassinated; More Than a Dozen Knife Wounds

Around noon on the previous day, Kluff, a western patrol officer of the Customs Water Police, was patrolling the Suzhou Creek when he suddenly smelled a foul odor emanating from the water. He quickly shone a flashlight and saw a male corpse drifting downstream. The skin and flesh were gray-black and rotten. He pulled it up and examined it closely, finding that the corpse was naked and the clothes were completely decayed. There was still a rotten rope around the waist, and there were more than a dozen knife wounds all over the body. It was suspected that he had been assassinated and that a huge stone was tied to the corpse with a rope before it was sunk to the bottom of the river, what is known as "planting lotus flowers," in an attempt to cover up the crime. However, after the corpse was submerged for a long time, the rope gradually rotted, and the corpse broke free from the stone and floated to the surface. Therefore, it has been submerged in the river for several months. After the skin and flesh rotted, the face became blurred and unrecognizable, and it was difficult to estimate the age. The western patrol officer took the corpse to the police station and waited for the salvage bureau's patrol boat to take it to the bureau before reporting it for autopsy.

Arranging to See a Movie Leads to a Hotel; Claiming to Be Unmarried When He Has a Wife

Tang Dayuan, a woman from Pudong who lives on the upper floor of the Wanyuan Rice Store at No. 582 Kangti Road in the French Concession, is 23 years old this year. Recently, she has hired lawyers Wu Peng and Fang Junjie to represent her in filing a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special District, accusing Zhu Zhuocai (from Chongming, 25 years old), the younger brother of Zhu Zhuoying, the owner of the Wanyuan New Rice Store, of deceiving her into having an abortion. The complaint states that the plaintiff lives with her mother and stepfather on the upper floor of the store. Zhuocai, the younger brother of the store owner, often came to the store, and Zhang, Zhuoying's wife, introduced them, saying that he was not yet married. On the afternoon of the ninth day of the twelfth lunar month of the twenty-second year of the Republic of China, Zhuocai came and arranged to see a movie. The plaintiff believed him and went out with him. Unexpectedly, Zhuocai did not lead her to the cinema but forced her to the Yuebin Hotel on Fada Road, saying that they would wait a moment and then go to the movie. The plaintiff, unaware of anything unusual, followed him to Room 5, where she was raped three times. The plaintiff initially refused, but Zhuocai swore that he was not married and was willing to take her as his wife. After various deceptions and threats, she had to submit to his abuse. Who knew that she was secretly pregnant and her belly grew larger every day. She urged her sister-in-law to urge him to come and marry her, but initially, someone was sent to negotiate, and then the appointment was indefinitely postponed. On the third day of the fourth lunar month of this year, Zhang told the plaintiff to go, saying that her uncle already had a wife, and asked her to get an abortion pill from Yi Yiyuan to have an abortion to prevent people from knowing. The plaintiff brought the medicine back and was about to take it when her mother found out and interrogated her strictly, so she could only tell the truth. Her mother wanted to drive the plaintiff out, so someone ran to tell the plaintiff's aunt, who came home to persuade her. Later, Zhuocai asked Yuan to come and explain that 120 yuan would be paid as settlement, with 50 yuan paid first. The plaintiff's mother refused. On the twelfth day of the fourth lunar month, Yuan came again to pay 15 yuan, but the plaintiff's mother did not accept it, and she threw it down and left. Later, it was discovered that the abortion pill was purchased by Yuan on behalf of Zhang, who also used seductive words to incite her to go to Pudong for an abortion. The plaintiff did not agree. The first defendant, Zhu Zhuocai, committed Article 244 of the Criminal Law. The second and third defendants committed Article 307 of the Criminal Law, the crime of assisting in an attempted abortion. She requests that the court investigate and handle the matter according to the law. The court has approved the petition and summoned the defendants yesterday. Zhu Zhuocai and Yuan did not appear in court. Judge Xiong briefly questioned the plaintiff and ordered that the hearing be adjourned to summon the witnesses to the court for further investigation.

Victim Identifies Him; Wife and Brother Detained for Visiting;

Qiu Guiyuan's home at No. 3 Yukang Lane, Oujia Road, was broken into by several bandits around 1:00 AM the day before yesterday. The gun and photos were presented for inspection. One bandit said that he was a patrol officer and would shoot anyone who made a noise. The thief seeking treatment at the hospital was indeed one of the four thieves, and the two defendants in custody were not at the scene. According to Chen Zhou, who lived at No. 84 Tongzhou Road, she was playing cards at Qiu's house when she was robbed of two gold rings and 28 yuan in cash. The thief wearing a white cloth shirt and blue pants looked similar to one of the people in the photo, the Li in the hospital. Her husband said he was shot by a Zhang on his way home and that she knew nothing about the robbery. Li Shoubai said that he heard that his brother had been shot at a certain number on Gonghe Road, Zhabei, and that he sent him to Baolong Hospital for treatment. He did not know that his brother was a robber. He asked the court for a clear understanding. Judge Wu Zehan adjourned the case for seven days to wait for the defendant Li Shoutang to recover from his injuries before further investigation. Li Wang and Li Shoubai were each released on bail of 500 yuan. If they could not provide bail, they would be remanded in custody.

A Young Man Attempts Suicide at the Majestic Hotel 155

Consuming Lysol and Orange Juice, Room Service Discovers Him and Rushes Him to the Hospital

A traveler, dressed in a Western suit and shirt, with yellow shorts, arrived at the Majestic Hotel on Avenue Edward VII the night before last. The hotel clerk led him to room 320. He registered as Zhang Zhenhua, 18 years old, from Shangyu. That evening, he only made one phone call and did not go out, retiring to his room. Yesterday morning around 11:00 AM, he got up, washed briefly, and ordered a bottle of orange juice from the tea server. He didn't ask for anything else and then closed the door. The tea server found his actions suspicious and became wary, secretly observing him. Soon after, the tea server noticed a strong chemical smell emanating from inside the room. Fearing an accident, he knocked on the door, but it was locked from the inside. They managed to open the door and found the young man lying stiffly on the bed, his face pale, and liquid running from his mouth. Upon closer inspection, a bottle of Lysol was found on the table in the room, with only a small amount of liquid remaining. There was also a cup containing half a cup of orange juice. Smelling it, they found it also contained Lysol. It was then realized that he had poured Lysol into the orange juice and drank it in an attempt to take his own life. The tea server immediately reported to the hotel clerk, who then reported to the police. He was rushed to Renji Hospital for treatment in a taxi. Doctors at the hospital performed a gastric lavage, but it was not completely successful, and his condition remained critical. At the same time, police investigating the young man's background discovered that the name he had given was false. His real name was Jiang Yiquan, and his age and hometown were the same. He had previously worked as an employee of the Wah Cheng Tobacco Company's Ningbo branch and was currently unemployed. According to his friends, the reason for his suicide was likely due to financial difficulties and a hard life.

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus Announce Cooperative Measures for Production, Transportation, and Sales at Various Stations 156

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, in order to promote the connection between production, transportation, and sales, have issued "Outline of Cooperative Measures for Production, Transportation, and Sales Along the Line" and formulated "Organizational Regulations for the Production, Transportation, and Sales Cooperation Committee." The articles are recorded separately as follows:

Outline of Cooperative Measures 157

Article 1: This Bureau, in its position as a transporter, cooperates with both producers and sellers to form a chain of production, transportation, and sales, aiming to regulate supply and demand and develop the national economy. Article 2: Cooperation is based on the principle of fairness, with mutual respect for each other's authority and mutual protection of each other's legitimate interests as the main principles. Article 3: Cooperation is temporarily limited to within 100 kilometers on either side of the railway line. Article 4: The cooperating parties are, on one side, this Bureau (including stevedores and contracted freight car companies) and, on the other side, all producers, sellers, or agents of producers and sellers (such as transshipment companies and travel agencies) who trade with this Bureau, collectively referred to as consignors. Consignors are temporarily limited to those who transport large quantities of goods or transport important domestic products on this railway line. Article 5: The matters this Bureau engages in for cooperation are as follows: (a) Providing necessary equipment and special preferential treatment within a reasonable or possible range for large-volume freight transport; (b) Contributing packaging improvement methods to suit railway transportation for the production and sale of goods, in order to save costs and time; (c) Dispatching personnel to guide or handle transportation procedures on behalf of others in places where there is production and sale of large quantities of goods; (d) Seeking to introduce purchasing and sales of domestic products and introduce various latest production and sales methods; (e) Providing statistics on the supply and demand of goods in various places along the line; (f) Other matters beneficial to the cooperation of production, transportation, and sales. Article 6: This Bureau hopes that

Article 7: In order to realize the cooperation matters stipulated in this outline, a cooperation committee may be established, and its regulations shall be determined separately. Article 8: If there are any unfulfilled matters in this outline, they may be revised at any time. Article 9: This outline shall be implemented after being resolved by the Bureau Affairs Conference of the Railway Bureau and reported to the Ministry of Railways for record.

Organizational Regulations for the Committee 159

Article 1: The cooperative affairs of this committee shall be based on the "Outline of Cooperative Measures for Production, Transportation, and Sales Along the Railway Line" of this Bureau. Article 2: This committee shall be established at each station with a large volume of freight transportation on this railway line. Article 3: The organization of this committee is as follows: (a) One to three representatives from the Railway Bureau; (b) One representative each from each type of consignor with a large volume of freight transportation at each station; (c) One representative from the Chamber of Commerce at each station location. Article 4: The main duties of this committee are as follows: (a) Jointly inspect and study various cooperative matters at each station. During inspections, the Railway Bureau may designate other related personnel to participate; (b) Report the aforementioned facts to the Railway Bureau in the name of the committee; (c) Suggest improvements to various transportation and loading and unloading methods or equipment. Article 5: This committee shall execute its duties jointly by all members as a principle. When necessary, it may divide into shifts or entrust representatives to take on the tasks. Article 6: The Railway Bureau shall provide suitable office space and equipment for this committee. The expenses of each committee member shall be borne by themselves. Article 7: This committee may formulate detailed rules based on the special circumstances of each station, but they must comply with the provisions of the "Outline of Cooperative Measures for Production, Transportation, and Sales Along the Railway Line" and these regulations, and be approved or agreed upon by the Railway Bureau. Article 8: If there are any unfulfilled matters in these regulations, they may be revised at any time. Article 9: These regulations shall be implemented after being resolved by the Bureau Affairs Conference of the Railway Bureau and reported to the Ministry of Railways for record.

The Citizen Education Center Opens a Consumer Cooperative 160

To Distribute Goods Directly and Share Profits Among All Members

The Municipal Citizen Education Center, considering that citizens' daily necessities mostly rely on merchants who are bound to calculate profits and may not supply goods adequately, and that the oppression of the environment in terms of livelihood is most serious, while public awareness is scattered and lacks voluntary cooperative organizations, drafted simple rules for a consumer cooperative last month and submitted them to the Education Bureau for approval. Preparations began in mid-month, dividing it into one thousand shares at one yuan per share. Each member can subscribe to a maximum of one-tenth of the total amount, with one vote per person, not proportional to the number of shares, which is absolutely different from shareholders in a company. The direct distribution of goods and the sharing of profits among all members is the characteristic of the cooperative. Open accounts are merely a secondary matter. The full text of the simple rules is extracted below. If citizens are interested in joining, they can request a membership application form from the office.

Simple Rules of the Shanghai Municipal Citizen Education Center Consumer Cooperative (1) This center, in order to promote cooperative undertakings and facilitate citizens, organizes a consumer cooperative in accordance with cooperative methods, named the Shanghai Municipal Citizen Education Center Consumer Cooperative. (2) The business scope of the consumer cooperative is limited to the daily needs of citizens, such as food, stationery, cosmetics, etc. (3) Before having a suitable location, the consumer cooperative will be temporarily located within this center. (4) All members of the consumer cooperative must subscribe to shares, temporarily set at one thousand shares, with one yuan per share. Each subscription may not exceed one-tenth of the total amount. (5) The organization of the consumer cooperative is as follows: (a) The Members' Meeting is the highest authority in the cooperative, held once every six months, with one vote per person. (b) The Board of Directors, consisting of five directors, mutually elect one chairman and one treasurer to handle the daily affairs of the cooperative. (c) The Board of Supervisors, consisting of three supervisors, mutually elect one chairman to supervise the duties performed by the Board of Directors. They report the income and expenditure situation to the members at each regular meeting. (6) The directors and supervisors are elected by the Members' Meeting, with a term of one year and eligible for re-election. (7) The Members' Meeting is held once every six months, and a quorum of more than half of all members must be present to hold the meeting. When necessary, the Board of Directors and Supervisors or a proposal from more than two-tenths of all members may convene an extraordinary meeting. (8) If a member is unable to attend the Members' Meeting due to circumstances, they may entrust an agent, but a sealed power of attorney is required for it to take effect. (9) Detailed rules for the Board of Directors and Supervisors shall be formulated separately and implemented after being approved by the Members' Meeting. (10) Dividends and net profits of the consumer cooperative will be distributed once at the end of each January and July. The distribution method is as follows: A. Annual interest on dividends is 5%. B. Net profit, after paying dividends and employee compensation, will be divided into ten parts. Three parts will be used to replenish the public reserve fund of the consumer cooperative, and seven parts will be distributed to the members. (11) These simple rules will be approved by the Center Affairs Meeting of this center and submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau for approval and implementation.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Pays Attention to the Commercial Registration Law 164

Soliciting Opinions from Various Industries

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to all executive and supervisory committee members and various industry associations to solicit opinions on the Commercial Registration Law. The letter stated: The chamber previously believed that Article 681 of the Civil Code, which stipulates joint and several liability for partnerships, was inconsistent with the commercial situation in our country. It requested the Legislative Yuan to amend it to be apportioned by shares. After years of debate, it was not approved. Although the Chamber had gathered opinions from various industries and proposed a separate method for registering partnerships and withdrawals, the Yuan believed that the partnership organization could be remedied by another Commercial Registration Law. There were also discussions by the Commercial Law and Civil Law Committees on drafting Commercial Registration Law regulations, but it has not been promulgated for a long time, making it difficult to implement the registration method proposed by the Chamber. In June of this year, the current session of the Members' Congress again resolved to request the Legislative Yuan to enact and implement the Commercial Registration Law as soon as possible. Before the law is promulgated, the opinions of merchant groups should be solicited as much as possible. On the 23rd of this month, the Commercial Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan replied, stating that the committee is currently drafting the Commercial Registration Law and needs to investigate the commercial conditions in various places for reference. Committee member Huang Youchang has been assigned to go to Shanghai to investigate. It is hoped that your Chamber will provide assistance and introductions. In addition to sending Mr. Huang a copy of the opinions of various industries on the case of joint and several liability for partnerships for reference, please express your high opinions on the Commercial Registration Law as much as possible. The letter should be submitted to the Chamber for review and forwarded for reference.

Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives Petition the Shanghai Municipal Council 165

Requesting the Recall of the Order to Register Rickshaw Pullers

Representatives of the rickshaw pullers, Wang Dexi, and others, petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating that the newly established regulations for rickshaw pullers are all impossible and difficult to accept, and requested a reconsideration to show genuine relief. The various impossible situations for the rickshaw pullers are hereby represented below: "Regarding the registration and licensing of rickshaw pullers," the new regulations require rickshaw pullers to be examined by a doctor to ensure that they are physically fit and deemed qualified before a license is issued. However, rickshaw pullers are all poor people, and their bodies lack nutrition. Not only are older rickshaw pullers unlikely to be deemed physically fit, but even younger rickshaw pullers will not easily qualify. It is undeniable that the reason they are able to pull rickshaws is that the wheels are pneumatic rubber tires and they are driven on flat asphalt roads, making it easy to do the work. If only strong and healthy rickshaw pullers are required, it is feared that there will be very few. This is the first impossibility. Moreover, those who make a living by pulling rickshaws in the concession are living in poverty, and their numbers are close to 80,000. The number of licenses the Rickshaw Affairs Association plans to issue is limited to 40,000. The remaining rickshaw pullers will inevitably be eliminated and will inevitably suffer from unemployment. It is asked where they will be placed. This is the second impossibility. Other things, such as the provision that rickshaw pullers' licenses cannot be transferred, is even more shocking. Rickshaw pullers come and go, and there is no fixed number. Even those who pull rickshaws all year round work in shifts of 12 hours each. During that time, they may lack the strength, so sons often help their fathers pull, and younger brothers replace older brothers to allow them to rest. This has become commonplace. If licenses are not allowed to be transferred, the rickshaw being pulled will have to be stopped immediately, and where will the car rental fee be paid from? This is the third impossibility. Moreover, in the event of violations or unruly behavior by rickshaw pullers, the rickshaw owner and foreman are responsible, and the police and courts are responsible for punishment. It has been followed to this day, and there is no need for new regulations for registration and licensing. It has been found that there are 10,000 public rickshaws in the concession, and according to the rental regulations, there are 60 shifts per day and night, and each shift works less than 12 hours. A rickshaw puller cannot work more than 13 or 14 shifts per month at most. If a rickshaw puller is strong, they can pull for a maximum of 9 or 10 hours and cannot pull any longer. For the remaining hours, some physically unsound rickshaw pullers buy 2 or 3 hours from the full-shift rickshaw puller, called pulling the rickshaw's rear and a corner of the night. This is how the physically challenged rickshaw pullers make a living. It is estimated that there are 20,000 to 30,000 people, and including the rickshaw pullers on the full shift, there are indeed 70,000 to 80,000 people. Your bureau's regulations stipulate that only 40,000 rickshaw pullers can be registered. If the number of rickshaw pullers who fail to register exceeds 40,000, there are also rickshaw pullers' wives or one or two children under budget, and the actual number is more than 100,000 poor people, who all rely on pulling rickshaws to make a living. They have always been law-abiding, selling their labor, sparing no effort, and struggling to make a living. Fortunately, your bureau sympathized with their situation and established a Rickshaw Committee, 口口聲聲均以救濟車夫爲前提, One says to raise the position, and the other says to improve the life. The Technicians of the Commodity Inspection Bureau Invent Intestine Casing Bleaching Powder 167

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection and Production Group of the Ministry of Industry, in view of the fact that there are many intestine casing manufacturers in this port, and the number of products exported to foreign countries every year is very large, occupying a considerable position in international trade, but most of them stick to the old methods and do not do research. When there are preliminary problems, the follow-up is not good, and the animal intestines change color and cannot be saved. It is a pity that the valuable animal intestines are turned into useless waste. Not only does the factory's output decrease and money is lost, but it also has an impact on the country's international trade. Chen Jun Zilong, the intestine casing inspection technician of the group, worked hard during his spare time to study and try various chemical drugs in order to restore them to their original state, export them to foreign countries, increase the country's economic income, and eliminate unnecessary losses to merchants and factories. For more than half a year, it has been slightly effective. Later, with the guidance of Chen Shunyun, the director of the group, two kinds of intestinal casing bleaching powder were invented, one is intestinal casing bleaching liquid, and the other is intestinal casing bleaching powder. When the color of the intestinal casing is not good, you can use bleaching liquid to bleach it. If you are still not satisfied, add a little bleaching powder to it, and it will make it as fresh as intestinal casing. However, the tissue of the bleached intestinal casing is not damaged at all. This kind of medicine not only has the effect of bleaching intestinal casing, but also has the ability to prevent corrosion and disinfect, and has no hindrance to our health. It is no more than the intestinal casing made without this kind of medicine. Chen Jun Zilong has gone to various factories to test it, and the results are excellent. It is now heard that the bureau plans to report the situation to the Ministry of Industry and give it a patent.

Ban Marriage Agency 168

Reading Q&A

Scientific Rainmaking vs. Ritual Rainseeking (Continued) 181

丨丨Answer to Mr. Zhu Ming 丨丨

Ritual rainseeking is a superstitious act, which is something everyone with common sense knows. In today's world where science has developed to a high degree, superstitious acts are clearly a major obstacle to social progress, and those who support superstition clearly have a numbing effect. On the one hand, we have clearly seen that scientists around the world can use scientific methods to reliably create artificial rain, while on the other hand, we spend a lot of money and manpower to make useless prayers. This is really a strange thing in the world today!

Superstitious behavior is a custom among backward people and has a long and deeply rooted history. Rainseeking is one of these customs. The livelihood of the people depends entirely on farming, and the success of farming depends on the appropriate amount of rainfall. Rainfall is a matter of life and death for the people. In the feudal era when science was unknown, people did not understand how rainfall occurred and had to explain it with divine power. When rainfall did not occur for a long time, they used rainseeking rituals to flatter the gods they imagined. This was inevitable in the society of many years ago. However, after the rise of science, people can no longer entrust their fate to the will of ghosts and gods, but gradually learn to conquer nature themselves, so that everything in nature can benefit human life. Therefore, with the development of capitalism and the progress of science, superstitious behavior has gradually disappeared in human society. For example, in China, after the May Fourth Movement, some people gradually realized the importance of science and stood up to oppose superstition and theocracy. However, in recent years, especially this year, superstitious behavior has suddenly been promoted very universally. First, the Kalachakra Dharma Assembly was a big commotion, followed by the discovery of the scientific spirit planchette diagram, and recently the rainseeking, where living Buddhas, heavenly masters, and Catholics were all mobilized, almost making people suspect that they were born hundreds of years ago. Why is this? Is science really not working?

In fact, this matter is not accidental. Our current surroundings are not only full of the restoration movement of superstitious behavior, but also thickly filled with a nostalgic atmosphere. In schools, classical Chinese has replaced vernacular Chinese, and in social life, the teachings in the Four Books and Five Classics have been promoted again. Obviously, someone is trying to pull the people back to the living state of two thousand years ago. Under such circumstances, when drought is about to form, another superstitious behavior of rainseeking is inevitable. Therefore, although it is clear that the behavior of rainseeking is so boring, not only is there no opposition, but some people are vigorously promoting it, which is also one of the manifestations of using old customs to thicken the nostalgic atmosphere. (To be continued)
